Such smart environment data may be indicative of a status of environment or of a particular user of environment e.g. the availability of someone at environment to receive package PL whereby a delivery entity may be able to leverage such smart environment data for more efficiently attempting to deliver package PL.

Next at step process may include accessing smart environment data that may be associated with at least one of the recipient and the location of the order of step . Such smart environment data may include any suitable data indicative of a particular smart home environment and or user e.g. user UL or UR of that may be registered or otherwise associated with platform e.g. a smart entity . For example any smart environment e.g. smart home or other environment equipped with one or more smart devices that may be integrated with platform may be associated with any suitable environment platform identifier e.g. via address geographic coordinates unique environment ID etc. that platform may use to uniquely identify environment in any suitable way. Additionally or alternatively any system user e.g. person animal etc. that may be registered or otherwise associated with platform may be associated with any suitable user platform identifier e.g. via name address facial detection a registered personal mobile device unique user ID etc. that platform may use to uniquely identify that user in any suitable way. In some embodiments by leveraging the identification of the recipient and or location provided during placement of the order at step certain smart environment data may be accessed that may be associated with that recipient and or location e.g. any suitable user platform identifier of platform associated with that recipient as a known user of platform and or any suitable environment platform identifier of platform associated with that location as a known environment of platform . For example a facilitator entity such as a fulfillment entity that may facilitate the placement of the order and or a delivery entity that may facilitate the delivery of the order may communicate with platform in order to attempt to access such smart environment data e.g. if the recipient or location of the order matches any known user or environment of platform . As just one example such a facilitator entity may be a fulfillment entity e.g. Amazon.com or a delivery entity e.g. Federal Express and may be a business that may be operative to communicate with any other suitable portion of platform e.g. system via one or more APIs to access such smart environment data that may be associated with the recipient and or location of the order. As another example a fulfillment entity may also be a delivery entity e.g. a restaurant that receives an order prepares the meal content and then delivers e.g. on foot or bicycle or car the meal content in a package e.g. brown bag to environment . Alternatively or additionally the ordering entity that placed the order of step may provide the facilitator entity with suitable smart environment data e.g. a user platform identifier of platform associated with the recipient and or an environment platform identifier of platform associated with the location may be known to and shared by the ordering entity with a facilitator entity either during or after placement of the order at step . Alternatively or additionally the order placed at step may be at least partially enabled by a component or subsystem of platform e.g. of system that may be operative to provide the facilitator entity e.g. fulfillment entity and or delivery entity with suitable smart environment data associated with the order e.g. a user platform identifier of platform associated with the recipient and or an environment platform identifier of platform associated with the location of the order may be known to and shared by system with a facilitator entity e.g. via API either during or after placement of the order at step .

At step process may include generating unique package identification information e.g. unique invitation identification information based on the accessed smart environment data and at least one of the content the recipient and the location of the ordered package and or a facilitator of the ordered package. For example if a smart environment and or a user of platform e.g. a smart system entity is associated with the location and or recipient of the ordered package such that smart environment data indicative of that smart environment and or user may be accessed at step unique package identification information may be generated at step that may identify that smart environment and or that user of platform e.g. using the smart environment data and or at least one identifier of the ordered package e.g. the content the recipient the location and or a facilitator fulfiller deliverer entity that may be at least partially responsible for delivering the package etc. . Such unique package identification information may be generated by any suitable entity such as by system and or a business facilitator entity and may be shared with any other suitable entity or entities e.g. with system by facilitator entity and or with facilitator entity by system . For example in some embodiments system may associate smart environment data of a smart system entity e.g. an environment and or user U with at least one of a recipient or location of a placed order and may generate unique package identification information for that order using the smart environment data and any suitable identifier s of that order and then may share that unique package identification information with a facilitator of the order e.g. a delivery entity charged with delivering the ordered package . Alternatively in some embodiments a business that may facilitate the order e.g. a retail entity or a delivery entity may access smart environment data when at least one of the recipient and location of an order is associated with a smart system entity of system and then business may generate unique package identification information for that order using the smart environment data and or any suitable identifier s of that order e.g. recipient deliverer orderer contents location etc. where such unique package identification information may be shared by facilitator business with system or any other suitable portion of platform e.g. a confirmation number generated by such a facilitator entity for a specific order e.g. a unique order confirmation number may be leveraged as such unique package identification information .

Process may include a facilitator obtaining at step a current status or mode setting of a smart system entity e.g. an environment and or user U of the smart environment data that may be associated with the unique identification information of the ordered package and then at step altering delivery of the ordered package based on the obtained status. That is when a smart environment and or a user U of system e.g. a smart system entity may be associated with a placed order e.g. as a location and or recipient of the order such that unique package identification information may be generated that links that environment or user with the placed order the handling of that order may be affected by any suitable characteristic of that environment or user. For example after an order for a package is placed e.g. at step but before that ordered package is delivered e.g. at step a current status or characteristic of at least one smart system entity associated with the ordered package as may be determined through leveraging platform and unique package identification information e.g. at step may be obtained by a facilitator for altering the delivery of the package.

As just one example when a facilitator delivery entity is about to deliver the ordered package e.g. when the ordered package is received at a distribution center proximal to the location from a remote originating distribution center the delivery entity may leverage the unique package identification information of the package to obtain current status information of a smart system entity associated with the package e.g. associated with the unique package identification information from platform e.g. system in order to determine how to most efficiently deliver the package. In some embodiments e.g. after step and or prior to step the unique package identification information may be incorporated into data e.g. code data or NFC data of a shipping label that may be affixed to or otherwise associated with the package e.g. label ID of package PL of and such a label may be scanned by the delivery entity in advance of an actual delivery attempt of the ordered package e.g. at step so as to enable the delivery entity to obtain current status information about the ordered package from platform . Such status information may be dynamic and change over time e.g. after step but before step such that the facilitator entity may obtain current status information before attempting to deliver the package in order to efficiently deliver the package based on the most useful status information. For example a deliverer of delivery entity business may first access and leverage the unique package identification information of a package to obtain current status information prior to a deliverer of delivery entity business arriving at environment with the package. As shown in for example a deliverer agent DR at a dispatch center DC of business remote from location LU of environment may utilize label ID of package PL to access and leverage the unique package identification information of package PL to obtain current status information prior to business instructing deliverer agent DL of to arrive at door of environment with package PL.

Status information regarding a smart system entity e.g. a smart environment or user U may be any suitable information generated by or inferred from any suitable data of platform e.g. of sensors of environment and or from user U . As just one particular example as mentioned above system may use tracking information to make inferences regarding the current and or future occupancy of home environment and or the current and or future location of a user U e.g. at environment like user UL of and Husband of or away from environment like user UR of and Wife of where such current and or future occupancy inferences may be obtained as current status information and then may be leveraged by a facilitator to affect the delivery of the package e.g. to delay delivery until a time when environment may be occupied by the recipient to receive the delivery . As another example system may be configured to enable a user U to access information about any ordered packages that may be associated with that user e.g. packages to be delivered to that user as a recipient or to that user s smart environment as a location which may be determined through identifying any unique package identification information that may be associated with that user or an environment of that user e.g. with an applicable smart system entity such that the user may manually update any settings that he or she may wish to have be associated with any such ordered package e.g. for affecting its delivery . For example using a device a user may interface with any suitable user interface that may be provided by any suitable entity of platform e.g. system to dictate and or edit any status information that may be associated with an ordered package and then used by a facilitator business for efficiently delivering that package such as altering the delivery location e.g. target at which the package ought to be delivered or defining a particular time during which the delivery should or should not be made to the location and the like. Therefore the status information that may be obtained by a facilitator e.g. a deliverer at step may be indicative of the actual current status of a smart system entity e.g. a smart environment or user U at that moment and or of a future status of that smart system entity e.g. during what future times environment is expected to be occupied and during what future times environment is expected to not be occupied etc. and such status information may be based on inferences or other processing that may be automatically carried out by platform e.g. system based on any suitable sensed data with respect to any smart system entity e.g. by any smart sensing devices of environment and or based on any manual instructions or settings defined or otherwise provided by a system user to platform e.g. to a smart device and or to system .

A do not disturb mode may be set for a particular environment or at least a portion thereof for any suitable length of time that may start at a current or future moment. Such a mode may indicate that environment may not be willing or able to accept at least certain package deliveries e.g. deliveries requiring a confirmation of receipt user signature by a particular user or any user . Such a mode may be manually set by an appropriate user e.g. a user with appropriate management rights for environment using any suitable device or interaction with any other suitable smart device of environment or any other suitable component of system of platform for any suitable reason such as when the user does not want to greet a visitor e.g. if the user is feeling under the weather or going to sleep or when the user will not be at environment e.g. when the user is going on vacation or leaving a babysitter at home with a child . Alternatively platform may be operative to collect any suitable information from one or more smart devices of environment and may make inferences in order to automatically set a do not disturb mode for environment e.g. based on sensed occupancy data and sensed movement data .

Information indicative of when environment may be associated with such a mode may be a type of current status information that may be associated by platform with unique package identification information and shared with or otherwise made accessible to a facilitator entity e.g. a delivery business for increasing the efficiency of package delivery and or of any other activity that may include a visitor interacting with environment . Such information may be handled with sensitivity so as to not be leveraged for sinister purposes e.g. for a third party to detect when an environment is in a do not disturb mode so as to assume no one is home and attempt a robbery of the premises . System may be configured to share information about a do not disturb mode of an environment or any other suitable status information of environment or a user thereof with a third party such as a facilitator of a package delivery only when certain data is accessible to that third party. For example system may only share such status information when a facilitator entity queries system with respect to particular unique package identification information e.g. such information as may be generated at step and linked with a particular ordered package . Certain facilitator entities e.g. Federal Express may be trusted and enabled by platform to interpret such unique package identification information for appropriately querying system about such status information and whereby system may be configured to only share such status information when queried by a trusted entity e.g. when the unique package identification information is known by or otherwise leveraged by an entity e.g. a deliverer entity trusted by system and not just when any entity has access to the recipient and or location data of the ordered package .

Status information of a smart system entity associated with unique package identification information of an ordered package may include various types of information that may be obtained and leveraged e.g. at steps by a facilitator entity for delivering the package in a manner that may be more efficient for the facilitator entity and or that may be more convenient for environment or a user thereof. For example such status information may include information indicative of when to allow delivery to a particular location e.g. after 4 00 PM on Mondays and Wednesdays only at environment information indicative of preferred alternate delivery methods e.g. do not deliver to environment but rather hold a particular package at a particular deliverer pick up location for manual pick up by a particular user or deliver to another recipient and or to another location other than the recipient and or location initially defined at step information indicative of authorization to deliver without signed confirmation of receipt of delivery e.g. a particular authenticated user of the system hereby authorizes deliverer to deliver a particular package to a particular location and leave next to the front door of that location without a human user signing for that delivery and or any other suitable information indicative of any other suitable delivery preferences or delivery instructions. For example in response to receiving status information indicative of authorization to deliver to another location the facilitator may be operative to obtain status information associated with a smart environment of that other location e.g. for repeating one or more steps of process with respect to that smart environment .

In some embodiments status information may be provided to a facilitator on a macro level in addition to or as an alternative to providing status information with respect to just one particular environment and or user thereof. For example status information may be made available to a facilitator entity business that may be generally indicative of a status or trend of a particular group of smart system entities e.g. a neighborhood or ZIP code that may include multiple smart environments that may include a smart system entity identified based on certain package information. As just one example such status information may be indicative of certain days of the week or other suitable current or future periods when a majority or any suitable threshold amount of environments of a group of environments including an environment associated with certain package information are not available to receive packages and such information may be leveraged by the facilitator entity to avoid scheduling deliveries to that entire group e.g. neighborhood of environments during those days. Any suitable grouping of environments or users or other suitable smart system entities of any suitable size and type may be used to generate group or macro level status information that may be made available to a facilitator entity for more efficiently handling business e.g. deliveries associated with that group. By grouping smart system entities and only sharing status data at a group level with third parties such as facilitator entities platform may protect the privacy and or security of certain environments by not sharing status information associated specifically with only a particular single environment e.g. to preserve at least some anonymity about the status of a particular smart environment .

By accessing certain status information of a smart environment or other suitable smart system entity of platform as may be detected or inferred by system a facilitator entity business may be configured to optimize package delivery. For example data indicative of when a particular location may and may not be able to receive a package delivery may be processed by any suitable distribution system to dictate when certain packages are dispatched for maximizing the likelihood of a successful physical delivery. In some embodiments when status information is obtained at step indicative of current availability of a target environment to receive a package e.g. availability for the next 4 hours facilitator may immediately deliver the package to environment yet in other embodiments when status information is obtained at step indicative of no current availability of a target environment to receive a package e.g. not available for at least the next 4 hours facilitator may delay the delivery of the package to environment e.g. until new status information may be obtained at a later use of step . As another example in some embodiments when status information is obtained at step indicative of an instruction to deliver a package to an initial target environment that is currently available to receive the package e.g. availability for the next 4 hours facilitator may immediately deliver the package to environment yet in other embodiments when status information is obtained at step indicative of an instruction to deliver a package to a new target environment rather than an initial target environment facilitator may repeat one or more of steps with respect to smart environment data associated with that new target environment . This may reduce overhead costs for a delivery entity e.g. reduce fuel prices and wasted man hours by limiting the number of failed delivery attempts and or may reduce insurance costs by limiting the exposure of perishable contents from unnecessary and degrading delivery effects.

One some or all of steps and may be at least partially or completely automated using one or more computer systems e.g. computer system and or computer system that may be leveraged by one or more of environment system facilitator entity business and the like for automatically associating a smart system entity of system with an ordered package and then sharing certain status information of that smart system entity with a deliverer or other facilitator entity at any suitable time for positively affecting the delivery of the package. A user of system may actively and manually define certain preferences or instructions to be shared with facilitator entity businesses for affecting the delivery of a particular ordered package currently associated with that user or for affecting the delivery of any package that may be associated with that user in the future. Alternatively or additionally the delivery of ordered packages associated with a user or environment may be based on inferences made by system and selectively shared with facilitator entity businesses e.g. without any active manual preferences made by the user but instead done transparently to a user . Therefore in some embodiments once an order is placed at step one some or all of steps may be carried out transparently to a system user e.g. to a recipient of package PL by platform based on any status information that may be determined automatically by system and or based on previously defined settings made by a system user.

It is understood that the steps shown in process of are merely illustrative and that existing steps may be modified or omitted additional steps may be added and the order of certain steps may be altered.

When delivery of an ordered package is actually attempted at a smart environment whether or not in accordance with process one or more smart devices of environment may be leveraged to at least partially automate the handling of the delivery attempt which may increase the efficiency of the delivery attempt and or to minimize any inconvenience to a user of environment that such a delivery attempt may cause. For example an entryway interface device such as a smart doorbell may be provided at a suitable entryway of a suitable portion of a smart environment for initiating or otherwise facilitating interaction between a delivery entity and smart environment that may efficiently handle a package delivery attempt e.g. to reduce delivery failures to increase user satisfaction and convenience and or to minimize risk of package theft .

According to some embodiments one or more sensing components or other suitable components of doorbell in combination with rules based inference engines or artificial intelligence or any other suitable processing components of platform provided at a central server such as system or otherwise may be used to detect when a package is attempted to be delivered to smart home environment and to take a variety of automated actions in response. For example sensing components may be operative to see the uniform of a delivery person approaching doorbell or the truck of the delivery person or the sensors can hear a delivery drone or hear a delivery truck in combination with footsteps of a delivery person approaching the door within a period after hearing the truck. Once the deliverer is within a predetermined distance from the door or entry point that may be associated with smart doorbell doorbell may be configured to ask the suspected deliverer e.g. using speaker if he or she is a delivery person to which that person can reply with an audible response or by indicating as such on user interface of doorbell . If the person is making a delivery doorbell can be configured to instruct the person to place the package in a suitable location proximate doorbell such that its scanner or any other suitable sensing component can scan the bar code or other type of identifying tag affixed to or associated with the package being delivered for detecting suitable package identification information.

According to embodiments a central server such as system can use the bar code or any suitable data detected directly from the deliverer or local package to obtain information about the package such as the sender recipient a description of the item therein whether signature is required etc. Based on this information rules based inferences engines or artificial intelligence or otherwise of platform may be operative to make one or more inferences regarding any action to take next. For example if occupants or more particularly if a specified recipient or recipients are in the home and the package is from a sender or contains an item that is of particular interest to the one or more occupants an announcement can be made in the home indicating the package is currently being dropped off and providing details about the package. On the other hand if the sender or item is not of particular interest to one of the occupants based on the occupants past responses to receiving such deliveries then no announcement may be made and the occupants can discover the package in due course. Similarly if no occupants are home but an inference is made that the package is of particular interest to one of the occupants a text message e mail telephone call or any other suitable contact attempt can be made to the one or more identified occupants indicating that the package is being delivered.

According to embodiments in the event a signature may be required for the package but none of the occupants are home or available to interface with the deliverer to provide such a signature an inference may be made not to disturb the occupants and doorbell can be configured to provide authorization to the deliverer to leave the package. For example doorbell may be operative to present an authorization code e.g. in plain text barcode or encrypted forms via any suitable output component of doorbell and may prompt the deliverer to use a deliverer device to record scan photograph or otherwise acquire the authorization code. Once the authorization code has been acquired by the deliverer doorbell can then instruct the deliverer regarding how to properly leave the package at environment such as at the front door around the back of the house in a discrete location etc.

Such detected package identification information of step may be unique package identification information that may be initially generated or at least partially defined by system of platform based on smart environment data of a smart system entity associated with the package prior to the delivery attempt e.g. as described above with respect to step of process where such smart unique package identification information may be detected by doorbell directly from deliverer DL or device of deliverer DL and or from package PL e.g. from label ID . Alternatively such detected package identification information of step may be conventional package identification information such as handwritten addressee information that may be manually entered on a shipping label ID of the package by a human or any other conventional delivery shipping label information. In some embodiments the delivery attempt may be for a package that does not include any shipping label ID at all. For example package PL may simply be a plate of cookies that a friendly neighbor has made and is attempting to deliver as deliverer DL to an occupant of environment . In such embodiments the information associated with the package that may be detected by doorbell may be captured image data of deliverer DL and or package PL e.g. as may be captured by a camera sensing component of doorbell spoken word data as may be provided by deliverer DL describing the delivery of package PL e.g. as may be captured by an audio sensing component of doorbell textual data as may be entered by deliverer DL describing the delivery of package PL e.g. as may be captured by a keyboard user interface input component of doorbell or any other suitable data that may be detected by doorbell via any suitable data path regarding deliverer DL and or package PL.

Doorbell may be configured to detect any suitable package identification information at step in any suitable way such as by instructing a detected deliverer DL to share such information e.g. by instructing deliverer DL to position an appropriate portion of package PL e.g. label ID in an appropriate location e.g. using any suitable output component of doorbell or other smart device such that a sensing component of doorbell may be able to access information therefrom or doorbell may be configured to automatically detect any suitable package identification information without requiring any specific activity on behalf of the deliverer DL e.g. doorbell may automatically detect suitable package identification information whenever a deliverer DL arrives with package PL within a particular distance of doorbell e.g. via NFC or RFID or Bluetooth technology . When deliverer DL or package PL is detected by doorbell either in response to a deliverer actively identifying itself or the package to doorbell or in response to doorbell automatically identifying the deliverer and or the package certain types of information may be accessed for analysis by environment e.g. time and date of attempted delivery identification of deliverer recipient content of package any delivery requirements etc. .

At step process may include analyzing the detected visitor information e.g. the detected package identification information of step e.g. in conjunction with any other suitable data available to platform such as settings of a current mode of environment or of a user . For example in response to detecting such package identification information at step with respect to deliverer DL and or package PL doorbell alone or in combination with other smart devices and or rules based inference engines and or artificial intelligence provided locally at environment and or in conjunction with system and or any other component s of services platform e.g. business may be operative at step to access any suitable additional information based on that detected package identification information that may be useful e.g. identification of the sender intended recipient intended delivery location deliverer description of the contents of package PL whether signature is required to complete the delivery etc. and or any other suitable data available to platform e.g. setting information of a current mode of environment and or of a system user and then to analyze all such available information for determining whether or not to take one or more of a variety of automated actions based on that detected package identification information and or any additionally accessed information.

Certain package identification information may be directly determined by doorbell from any suitable initial data provided by deliverer DL and or package PL e.g. via data communication paths or while other package identification information may be accessed by doorbell from other sources based on such initial data e.g. from service and or business via service . For example a unique code that may be scanned by doorbell from label ID at package PL may be a unique identifier that doorbell may share with service such that service may access particular types of data associated with that identifier e.g. recipient content etc. from facilitator business . Alternatively such particular recipient and content data may be locally obtained by doorbell directly from package PL or deliverer DL e.g. via path from device which may or may not be accessing such data from server data of business via internet .

Current status information of a smart system entity associated with the package delivery which may be similar to the status information that may be obtained by a deliverer at step may be obtained and analyzed at step . Whether or not a facilitator entity may be configured to or otherwise allowed to obtain current status information of a smart system entity associated with package PL e.g. at step environment e.g. in conjunction with system may be configured to obtain and utilize such current status information at step in response to detecting certain package identification information at step where such status information may have been actively defined by a user of system or inferred or artificially generated by system for all deliveries generally or for a specific package delivery.

Any rules or instructions that may be obtained generated or otherwise determined by platform e.g. environment and or system at step based on the detected package identification information of step may be leveraged in any suitable way for positively affecting the delivery attempt of package PL. Once all available and accessible package data associated with the package delivery attempt has been obtained by environment e.g. package information obtained directly by doorbell from package PL and or deliverer DL and or any additional package information obtained via system based on any initial package information obtained by doorbell environment e.g. in combination with system may analyze that package data in combination with any suitable smart environment data or rules or settings or inferences or modes that may be associated with environment or any user or other smart system entity that may be associated with the package data and or with environment so as to determine one or more ways in which to efficiently handle the delivery attempt of package PL at doorbell . Such smart environment data that may be analyzed or processed in conjunction with any package data and or visitor deliverer data may include any suitable data associated with a smart environment user e.g. a user that has been identified as an intended recipient of the package or any other user associated with environment and or any suitable data associated with the smart environment itself such as the current and or anticipated future location of the smart environment user e.g. location within environment or outside of environment such as with respect to geo fences e.g. the user is currently driving towards environment and will arrive at environment within 2 minutes so as to receive the package the current and or anticipated future status or mode of a smart environment user e.g. sleeping busy on the telephone etc. the current and or anticipated future mode of the environment or user e.g. a do not disturb mode etc. and the like. Any suitable smart environment data described herein with respect to any smart device of environment or in conjunction with any other feature of platform e.g. system and or third parties and or extrinsic information and or processing paradigms may be analyzed or otherwise processed at step in conjunction with any package information that may be associated in any way with a package delivery attempt detected at step in order to initiate or otherwise prompt e.g. with doorbell and or other suitable components of environment and or platform any suitable action s for positively affecting the handling of a visitor e.g. the delivery attempt of package PL e.g. at one or more of steps of process . In some embodiments as soon as a deliverer DL is detected doorbell may be operative to indicate to deliverer DL that doorbell button is disabled e.g. to prevent deliverer DL from even bothering to try to contact an occupant through interaction with button . In some particular embodiments as described below in more detail doorbell may be operative to indicate that doorbell button is disabled in order to prevent any visitor from even bothering to try to contact an occupant through interaction with button at least until certain visitor detection and analysis has been completed by system .

At step process may include adjusting the functionality of at least one smart device of environment based on the analysis of step or even based solely on the detection of step . As just one example when a visitor is detected at step smart environment may be operative to turn on a light e.g. outdoor lighting to increase the safety of the visitor and or to increase the security of environment . As another example when a visitor is detected at step smart environment may be operative to emit any suitable sound e.g. a dog bark or a greeting from any suitable smart device e.g. from audio speaker of doorbell to increase the awareness of the visitor with respect to environment . As another example when a visitor is detected at step smart environment may be operative to lock any unlocked entry ways to structure e.g. by locking smart doorknob to increase the security of environment .

At step process may include communicating with a user associated with the smart environment based on the analysis of step . As just one example when the analysis of step determines that an intended recipient of package PL is a user that is currently located at environment and is in an active and available state e.g. not sleeping on the telephone or in any another do not disturb state as may be determined by smart environment smart environment may be operative to communicate information indicative of the current package delivery attempt to that user in any suitable way at step e.g. by audibly announcing any suitable information related to the delivery attempt of the particular package via an audio speaker of a smart device that may be located most proximal to the current location of that user within environment . As another example when the analysis of step determines that an intended recipient of package PL is a user that is not currently located at environment smart environment may be operative to communicate information indicative of the current package delivery attempt to that user via system in any suitable way at step e.g. by transmitting an electronic message to a personal device associated with that user .

In response to such communication by environment to a user the user may communicate in any suitable way a response back to environment e.g. via any suitable smart device e.g. hazard device or device to any suitable component of environment or system where such communication may be indicative of how the user would like environment to handle the detected delivery attempt. For example the user may instruct any suitable device of environment that the user does not wish to directly interface with the deliverer but that the delivery should be completed or carried out in some particular automated manner by environment and the deliverer. As another example the user may communicate to environment that the user will interface with the deliverer locally whereby the user may move towards entry point for physically interacting with deliverer DL to receive package PL. As yet another example the user may communicate to environment that the user will interface with the deliverer remotely via one or more devices of environment or system whereby environment may enable the user to communicate via a first smart device e.g. a hazard device of environment that may be proximate to user UL local to environment or a personal device of user UL or UR whether the user is local to or remote from environment and whereby environment may enable deliverer DL to communicate via a second smart device e.g. doorbell or other suitable device of environment such that the interconnectivity of those devices of environment may facilitate effective communication between the user and the deliverer. In certain embodiments by facilitating communication with an appropriate user via environment and system rather than requiring a deliverer to attempt to contact a user independently e.g. via a telephone number that may be associated with the ordered package e.g. at step process may reduce the burden of the deliverer while also retaining certain privacy of the user by utilizing system as an intermediary between the user and the deliverer such that certain types of contact information or ways of communicating with the user are guarded and protected by system and not necessarily shared with the deliverer while still enabling communication between the deliverer and the user via such ways of communication. That is whether or not a user is local to environment system may enable communication between the user and the deliverer without sharing the whereabouts or contact information of the user with the deliverer. A user may communicate with system via any suitable communication enabled by a smart device of environment when the user e.g. user UL is local to environment e.g. via gestures as may be described above with respect to smart device via touch input via a touch user interface audible spoken commands etc. and or via any suitable communication enabled by a system when the user is local to or remote from e.g. user UR environment e.g. via a user device .

At step process may include providing the visitor e.g. the deliverer with feedback based on at least one of the analysis of step and any communication of step . As just one example when the analysis of step determines that there are currently no occupants local to environment or otherwise in an active and available state and or when no user response is received for any communication attempt of step system may be operative to determine that smart environment may handle the attempted delivery without active user input and doorbell may provide the deliverer at step with instructions or other suitable feedback on how to proceed with the delivery. Alternatively when the analysis of step determines that there is a user local to environment that is in an active and available state and or when a user response is received for any communication attempt of step system may be operative to determine that a user of smart environment may at least partially handle the attempted delivery and doorbell may provide the deliverer at step with instructions or other suitable feedback on how to proceed with the delivery. The type of feedback that may be provided via doorbell to the deliverer at step may vary based on the analysis of step and or any communication of step . For example the feedback may include active communication from the user to the deliverer via doorbell e.g. audio and or visual or other suitable information may be conveyed to the deliverer by doorbell where such information may be generated and transmitted by or otherwise under the control of the user via another smart device that the user may directly interface with and that may be communicatively coupled to doorbell . Alternatively the feedback may include automated instructions generated by system for communication to the deliverer via doorbell e.g. a message that may communicate that a user is not currently able to actively receive the package right now please do the following to complete the delivery . . . etc. . Additionally or alternatively the feedback may include providing certain environment access to the deliverer such as by opening door by unlocking doorknob for a certain amount of time e.g. if deliverer DL is approved by system as an expected and or authorized deliverer e.g. through analysis of a label ID door may be unlocked such that deliverer DL may be enabled to enter structure for delivering package PL within structure . In some embodiments a deliverer device may be operative to be communicatively coupled with a smart device of environment and feedback may be communicated by such a smart device to deliverer device for receipt by the deliverer via an output of deliverer device e.g. device may be communicatively coupled with a communication component via path e.g. paired via BlueTooth or any other suitable protocol and such feedback may be communicated via path and then provided to the deliverer via any suitable output component of device .

At step process may include detecting an act of the visitor e.g. an act of the deliverer with the package based on the provided feedback of step e.g. an act performed by the visitor in response to the provided feedback . Doorbell and or any other smart device of environment may be configured to detect an action of deliverer DL and or package PL at step in response to system providing deliverer DL with feedback at step where that action may be any suitable action indicative of deliverer handling package PL in a particular way. As just one example in response to instructing deliverer DL to leave package PL at a particular location e.g. within a detection range of a sensing component of doorbell at step doorbell may detect such placement of package PL at step . As another example in response to requesting that deliverer DL deliver package PL to a neighboring environment e.g. to a next door neighbor of environment that may also be equipped with a smart doorbell at step doorbell of environment may detect a confirmatory response provided by deliverer DL that the request will be followed e.g. directly from deliverer DL at a user interface component of doorbell or from deliverer device via path at a communications component of doorbell or a confirmatory communication by a smart device of the neighboring environment that may confirm receipt of the package . Any suitable action of deliverer DL and or of package PL may be detected or otherwise received by any suitable component of environment and or of system at step where such detection may enable system to update system information about the status of the attempted delivery e.g. successfully delivered at front door successfully delivered to neighbor ABC to be re delivered at time XYZ etc. . Alternatively or additionally a deliverer DL may communicate with system at step via any suitable communication enabled by a smart device of environment accessible by deliverer DL e.g. via gestures at doorbell as may be described above with respect to smart device via touch input via a touch user interface audible spoken commands etc. and or via any suitable communication enabled by system and deliverer device .

At step process may include communicating with at least one of the user and the visitor e.g. the deliver based on the detected act of step . Doorbell and or any other smart device of environment may be configured to confirm detection of an action of deliverer DL and or package PL with deliverer DL e.g. by communicating any suitable confirmation information directly to deliverer DL or to delivery device via doorbell or to delivery business via system of platform . Alternatively or additionally doorbell and or any other component of environment and or system may be configured to confirm detection of an action of deliverer DL and or package PL with a user of environment e.g. by communicating any suitable confirmation information to the user via any suitable smart device or personal device of the user similarly to any communication of step . This may enable deliverer DL and or the user to remain updated with respect to the current status of the attempted delivery as determined by environment of system e.g. successfully delivered at front door successfully delivered to neighbor ABC to be re delivered at time XYZ etc. . Such communication of step may enable deliverer DL to know whether or not any action performed at step was successfully detected by system thereby removing any doubt about the status of the delivery. This may also create an electronic receipt or trail of the attempted delivery not only for the particular deliverer DL and or a user of environment but also any other interested party such as a management system of a delivery entity or fulfillment entity business . By such confirmation of delivery status being electronically or otherwise generated by system rather than by delivery entity business the confirmation may be considered even more reliable or leveraged in combination with any similar confirmation data that may be generated by delivery business e.g. based on manual entry into delivery device by deliverer DL to ensure accurate delivery status is available to platform . By providing confirmation data indicative of a detected delivery action to deliverer DL e.g. via doorbell and or to delivery entity business e.g. via an API of platform system may serve as a secondary or impartial source of information regarding the delivery of packages carried out by delivery entity business . This may increase the efficiency and or effectiveness of delivery entity business and or may lower overhead costs e.g. insurance costs of delivery entity business as system may provide a new source of accurate and real time electronic data that may be made available to delivery entity business for use in managing its package delivery tasks while also not being as dependent on delivery data provided by its own deliverers DL. Moreover by providing confirmation data indicative of a detected delivery action to a user of environment e.g. via any suitable system user communication capability of platform a user may be able to have access to an up to date status of a package delivery while also being enabled to virtually communicate with a deliverer during a delivery attempt in a manner that is convenient and secure for the user and the deliverer.

One or more of steps of process may be repeated for a particular delivery attempt of a particular package or for any other visitor handling. For example in response to analysis at step of any package delivery information detected at step a user may communicate with the smart environment at step and that user communication may be shared with deliverer DL at step in response to which an action of deliverer DL may be detected by the smart environment at step and that detected action may be communicated back to the user at step in response to which the user may once again communicate with the smart environment at step based on that communicated detected action thereby repeating at least part of process . Therefore process may support a virtual conversation between deliverer DL and a user or service as an automated agent of the user.

It is understood that the steps shown in process of are merely illustrative and that existing steps may be modified or omitted additional steps may be added and the order of certain steps may be altered.

In some embodiments communication of certain package information to a user at step may equip the user with the ability to decide how the user may want the delivery attempt to be handled. For example the user may decide to go meet the deliverer at door for personally receiving the package or the user may remotely instruct the deliverer to leave the package at a certain location via a communication path supported by environment e.g. via doorbell and any other suitable device such that the user may actively determine at least a portion of the feedback that may be provided to the deliverer at step . Alternatively communication of certain package information to a user at step may not be successfully received by a user in time for the user to effectively respond for immediate use by system or such communication may not even be attempted e.g. if the user is known by system to be on vacation or otherwise or otherwise in a do not disturb mode where system may determine not to contact the user . In such embodiments system may be configured to determine and generate the feedback provided to the deliverer at step without any active input from the user. Such feedback may instead be automatically determined based on inferences or rules of platform e.g. system and or any restrictions that may be applicable to the particular delivery e.g. user signature required . For example feedback provided at step may include an instruction for deliverer DL to simply leave package PL at door or to deliver package PL to a neighbor or to re attempt the delivery at another time that may be specified e.g. a time that may be determined by system as when an appropriate system user is expected to be available at environment for receiving a delivery . However if a signature or any other suitable type of acknowledgment of receipt of the package is required in order to complete delivery e.g. as may be detected through the package information detected and analyzed at steps and feedback provided at step by doorbell may include certain data that may satisfy that receipt acknowledgment requirement. For example system may have access to any suitable trusted security information that may also be known by or validated by delivery business whereby use of such information by system within feedback provided to deliverer DL at step may be received and confirmed by delivery business as an acceptable form of waiver of responsibility or acknowledgment such that deliverer DL may be able to leave package PL at environment without actively receiving a signature of a user. For example doorbell may present an authorization code e.g. in plain text as any suitable code or encrypted forms on a user interface e.g. on a display as at least a portion of feedback at step and may prompt deliverer DL to use deliverer device to record scan photograph or otherwise acquire the authorization code for authentication and acceptance e.g. as a detectable act at step . Once the authorization code has been acquired and accepted by deliverer DL doorbell may be operative to then instruct deliverer DL with respect to where to leave package PL.

Communication between deliverer DL and a system user of system may include various types of conversation types. For example in some embodiments deliverer DL may specifically dictate when and how package PL will be delivered. As just one such example in response to system providing feedback to deliverer DL at step indicative of the fact that a user of environment is not available to actively communicate with deliverer DL for facilitating completion of the delivery deliverer DL may communicate information to system e.g. via doorbell at step that may be indicative of the fact that deliverer DL is going to return package PL to a suitable pick up location e.g. distribution center DC of business and that package PL will be available at that location for pick up by the user at a certain time. In response to such a communication from deliverer DL system may confirm receipt of that information to deliverer DL and or may share such information with a user at step . Such a situation may enable the user to be informed of the pick up status of the package PL in real time or as soon as the user is able to receive such a communication from system thereby allowing the user to conveniently swing by that pick up location to retrieve package PL on the user s way home to environment . As opposed to conventional practice where a deliverer leaves a paper notice on a user s front door indicating that the user missed the delivery attempt and that the user must bring that paper notice to the pick up center to retrieve the package system may immediately and automatically share such notification information with a user electronically e.g. via e mail or text messaging or any other suitable system communication with the user such that the user need not waste time by driving home to receive a paper notice only to turn right around and drive to the pick up location to retrieve the package . Such interaction between deliverer DL and system e.g. via doorbell and such interaction between system and a system user may not only increase the convenience for the user but may also increase the efficiency of deliverer DL e.g. by saving paper notices and removing doubt as to whether the notice will be received by the user . Moreover the automated communication of such notice information may be provided to a system user without requiring or even allowing direct communication between deliverer DL and the user thereby enabling system to remain a custodian of certain contact information and whereabouts information of the user.

As another example communication between deliverer DL and a system user of system may include two way communication. As mentioned a real time virtual two way conversation between a user and a deliverer DL at doorbell may be enabled by system . For example a user may communicate a request to system at step e.g. I am unable to come to the door to sign for the package what are my options that may then be provided by system to deliverer DL at step e.g. relayed as audio data from an audio sensing device at the user to audio output data from doorbell in response to which deliverer DL may provide a response with one or more options for the user e.g. you can sign for the package at a designated pick up location after 5 pm today or a neighbor can sign for the package now on your behalf that may be detected by system e.g. doorbell at step and relayed to the user at step after which the user may again communicate to deliverer DL with his decision.

Alternatively a delayed response virtual conversation between a user and a deliverer DL may be enabled by system . For example system may communicate to deliverer DL e.g. via doorbell at step that a user of environment is not available to actively communicate with deliverer DL for facilitating completion of the delivery. In response to such feedback deliverer DL may communicate information to system e.g. via doorbell at step that may be indicative of the fact that deliverer DL will re attempt to deliver package PL at environment tomorrow. In response to detection of such a communication from deliverer DL system may confirm receipt of that information to deliverer DL and may share such information with a user at step e.g. automatically or immediately after such detection . However at some later time that same day e.g. after deliverer DL and package PL have left environment a system user may actually digest that information as shared with it by system . In response thereto as opposed to allowing deliverer DL to re attempt delivery of package PL at environment the following day as currently planned the user may wish to retrieve package PL from delivery business that evening at dispatch center DC or the user may wish for deliverer DL to deliver package PL to the user s office rather than to environment or any other suitable change to the currently planned delivery strategy. Therefore system may be configured to enable the user to share such a desire with delivery business for systematically altering the delivery strategy. For example system may be operative to provide an intuitive application or user interface e.g. on the user s device or via any smart device of environment that may enable a user to select from any available options for altering the delivery strategy where such options may be known or otherwise determined by system based on the package information detected at steps and or based on any other suitable information that may be made available to system e.g. from delivery business via an API or otherwise . A user selected option may then be automatically communicated from system to delivery business for updating the planned delivery strategy of package PL thereby increasing the efficiency and or convenience of the delivery process.

Various types of feedback may be provided to deliverer DL by system e.g. via doorbell at step and responsive thereto deliverer DL may commit various types of acts that may be detected by system e.g. via doorbell at step for advancing the attempted delivery of package PL. In some embodiments platform e.g. environment and or system may be configured to enable secure drop off of package PL by deliverer DL at environment when a system user is unable to physically receive package PL from deliverer DL at environment e.g. when no user is at environment or when a user is at environment but currently unavailable for active package receipt e.g. when the user is sleeping or otherwise pre occupied or otherwise unfit to meet deliverer DL . Certain steps may be taken by system and or certain features of environment may be enabled so as to increase the security and reliability of such an unsupervised drop off otherwise such a drop off may not be approved by delivery business e.g. such an act may not meet insurance standards of business or may not be of interest to a user e.g. such an act may not meet the security interests of the user . For example platform e.g. system in conjunction with environment may be configured to enable a secure drop off of a package confirm such a drop off secure the package after such a drop off remind a user of the secured package enable authorized recovery of the secured package and confirm such authorized recovery for completing the delivery process.

In some embodiments an unsupervised drop off may be enabled when environment is configured with an ability to receive and retain package PL in a secure location that may be trusted by both deliverer DL and a system user. For example a certain secure area of environment may be temporarily made accessibly by system to deliverer DL e.g. by feedback at step such that deliverer DL may deposit package PL within that secure area e.g. at step for later retrieval by a trusted system user e.g. the intended recipient . Any suitable secure area may be provided by environment for this purpose. As one example structure may include a lobby not shown just beyond entry point door that itself may be separated by the remainder of structure by another locked door and system may be configured to temporarily unlock door e.g. via smart doorknob for granting deliverer DL temporary access to that lobby for depositing package PL therein. Such a lobby may be a shared lobby amongst multiple distinct tenants e.g. a shared lobby of a multi residence apartment building . In such embodiments the lobby may include an area that may otherwise be selectively accessible to mailmen e.g. via a shared key that Postal Service workers often times are equipped with in urban areas where large apartment buildings are common . Such temporary access as may be granted by system in response to suitable detection and analysis e.g. at steps and may overcome the need for certain deliverers to carry around one or more master keys for certain neighborhoods or apartment buildings which may also reduce security concerns for the building while increasing the efficiency and effectiveness of deliverers to securely deposit packages in areas of an environment that have at least a certain amount of security provided to it e.g. due to a front door of a lobby that is generally accessible only by trusted occupants of the building and not by any visitor attempting to gain access to the building . As another example a smart safe e.g. a smart appliance may be provided by environment adjacent doorbell external to structure e.g. smart appliance the interior of which may be selectively and temporarily made accessible to deliverer DL e.g. via any suitable control signals of system or environment e.g. via doorbell for enabling placement of package PL therein. Any such secure area e.g. a lobby a safe etc. of environment that may be made temporarily accessible to deliverer DL by system e.g. automatically through system processing and control may be securely monitored by platform during such temporary access in order to ensure that deliverer DL positions package PL in that area and or to ensure that nothing is removed from that area during the period of that temporary access. One or more sensing components of doorbell or of any other smart device of environment may be configured to at least partially carry out such monitoring e.g. a sensing component within the secure area or external to the secure area but that may sense activity within the secure area and or at the temporarily accessible opening to the secure area may be activated and or enhanced e.g. by platform during such temporary accessibility for securely monitoring the activity of deliverer DL during that accessibility . Additionally or alternatively one or more output components of doorbell or of any other smart device of environment may be configured to at least partially indicate to deliverer DL where and how to deposit the package securely.

System may require that a certain level of trust be achieved between platform e.g. environment and or system and deliverer DL before enabling such temporary access to such a secure area of environment . For example certain package delivery data may be retrieved and analyzed at steps and prior to enabling such an unsupervised drop off such as specific identification data of the particular deliverer DL and or of the particular package PL at doorbell that system may be able to confirm or cross check with a trusted delivery business e.g. via an API of platform between system and business . Therefore system may confirm the identity of deliverer DL and or package PL based not only on identification data that may be provided to system locally at environment e.g. via doorbell but also on data that may be provided to system from business remotely from environment e.g. via an API such that a visitor may not attempt to gain access to a secure area of environment by fraudulently purporting to be a deliverer associated with a trusted delivery entity business . Such confirmation by cross referencing locally obtained deliverer package identification data with known or expected whereabouts status data for a particular deliverer package may be utilized by system for any suitable situation at steps in order to improve the security of an attempted package delivery.

Once a suitable level of trust is determined by system for deliverer DL and or package PL such that system may be configured to enable an unsupervised drop off system may be operative to instruct deliverer DL e.g. via doorbell how to carry out such an unsupervised drop off. For example doorbell may be configured to audibly instruct deliverer DL as to where to find a secure drop off area that may be made temporarily accessible to the deliverer for securing package PL e.g. via audio speaker that may provide any suitable audio output such as a verbal instruction to open the safe just to the right of the front door place the package therein and then close the safe . Alternatively or additionally doorbell may be configured to visually instruct deliverer DL as to where to find a secure drop off area that may be made temporarily accessible to the deliverer for securing package PL e.g. via user interface and or projector display . During such instructing system may also control the secure area for enabling deliverer DL to have access thereto e.g. by unlocking a door to a safe .

Once deliverer DL is instructed how where to access a secure area and such a secure area is made temporarily accessible to deliverer DL e.g. at step system may be configured to securely monitor that secure area during the period when the secure area is made accessible e.g. by leveraging any suitable monitor sensing components of doorbell and or any suitable sensing components of the secure area itself or otherwise e.g. any cameras that may be provided by a smart safe appliance etc. . Such monitoring may be leveraged not only to confirm that a particular package PL is secured within the secure area but also to confirm that nothing is removed from the secure area. For example one or more sensors of environment may be configured to detect label ID or any other suitable identifier of package PL intermittently and or continuously during the process of placing package PL within the secure area such that system may detect and confirm that package PL has been positioned with the secure area e.g. steps and . Additionally or alternatively one or more sensors of environment may be configured to monitor the access point of such a secure area continuously during the process of placing package PL within the secure area such that system may confirm that nothing is removed from the secure area. Such confirmation of proper drop off of package PL may be shared with delivery entity business by system e.g. via API and or with deliverer DL e.g. via doorbell and or with a system user e.g. via a user device or any suitable smart device . Once the positioning of package PL has been confirmed within the secure area system may be configured to terminate the accessibility to the secure area e.g. by locking the door to the safe .

If no physically distinct secure area e.g. safe or lobby is available to environment system may enable proper drop off of package PL by designating a certain area of environment as an area at which package PL may be left and adequately securely monitored by system e.g. doorbell . For example at step rather than instructing deliverer DL towards a safe or lobby that may be temporarily made accessible to deliverer DL for depositing package PL system may leverage doorbell or any other suitable smart device of environment to instruct deliverer DL towards an open area at which deliverer DL may deposit package PL. As shown in one or more components of doorbell e.g. projector may be operative to generate and display to deliverer DL a suitable deposit area AL at which package PL may be dropped off e.g. light from projector may shine to identify area AL on any suitable surface or instructions provided on a display user interface or audible instructions via audio speaker may otherwise enable deliverer DL to identify the location of area AL . Area AL may be on a portion of a stoop or sidewalk or any other suitable portion of environment adjacent door or otherwise easily accessible to deliverer DL that may be securely monitored by environment e.g. by one or more sensing components of doorbell . For example area AL may be within a sensing range of an NFC or RFID or camera or any other suitable sensing component of doorbell such that when package PL may be positioned within area AL by deliverer DL package PL may be securely monitored by one or more smart devices of environment which may ensure secure drop off of package PL. As another example area AL may not be proximate doorbell but may be an area that may be monitored by another smart device of environment e.g. a smart device that may be coupled to outdoor lighting which may be around a corner of structure from front door such that other visitors to front door may not obviously notice package PL that has been deposited by deliverer DL for secure monitoring by environment . As with the deposit of package PL within any other suitable secure area e.g. a safe or lobby system may be configured to monitor and confirm the adequate deposit of package PL at area AL with deliverer DL and or delivery entity business for furthering the delivery attempt e.g. such that deliverer DL may confidently leave package PL at environment . Any suitable smart device of environment may provide and or monitor such an area AL or any other secure area for use in unsupervised drop off and monitoring of a package PL.

Alternatively or additionally system may enable proper drop off of package PL by providing an accessory device that may be coupled to package PL for enabling secure monitoring of package PL by system e.g. doorbell . For example at step rather than instructing deliverer DL towards a safe or lobby that may be temporarily made accessible to deliverer DL for depositing package PL system may leverage doorbell or any other suitable smart device of environment to instruct deliverer DL to couple an accessory component e.g. of doorbell of to package PL and then to leave package PL with accessory component near doorbell for secure monitoring. As shown in accessory component of doorbell may be coupled to package PL e.g. fastened adhered affixed snapped tied to rest on or otherwise attached where accessory component may be operative to communicate with or be detected by any other component s of doorbell e.g. communications component e.g. Bluetooth and or sensor component or any other suitable components of environment or platform when coupled to package PL such that platform may monitor the location and or any other suitable characteristic s of package PL e.g. based on the monitored location and or any other suitable characteristic s of accessory component . For example accessory component may be configured to include any suitable sensing components e.g. motion sensing components or any other suitable sensing components as described above with respect to sensing components that may detect movement or any other suitable characteristic of accessory component and thus package PL when coupled thereto and such sensed characteristics may be communicated to or otherwise detected by any other component s of doorbell and or any other suitable smart device of environment and thus system . Alternatively or additionally doorbell and or any other suitable smart device of environment may be operative to detect the location of accessory component such that if package PL is moved after deliverer DL leaves package PL e.g. by an animal or wind or otherwise doorbell and or any other suitable smart device of environment may be operative to track such movement for use in finding package PL for recovery. Such a physical coupling of package PL to a component of environment e.g. accessory of doorbell may increase the ability and or effectiveness of system to securely monitor a package during and after an unsupervised drop off Accessory component may be reusable anytime a new package is to be deposited for secure monitoring by doorbell and or any other suitable smart device of environment . As just one example accessory component may be an RFID tag that may be communicatively coupled or otherwise known by another component of doorbell . Any movement of package PL e.g. as may be detected through leveraging accessory component at all or above a certain threshold may trigger one or more additional sensing components of doorbell or otherwise of environment to monitor package PL component so as to heighten the secure monitoring of package PL. Accessory component may be operative to wirelessly communicate with other components of doorbell and or any other suitable smart device of environment and or may communicate via a wire that may extend between accessory component and other components of doorbell . If wire is cut or otherwise disrupted additional heightened security may be enacted by system to track package PL. In some embodiments a holder of doorbell and or any other suitable smart device of environment may be selectively opened and closed e.g. through electronic control of system for selectively enabling accessory component to be removed from the remainder of doorbell and or any other suitable smart device of environment for attachment to package PL.

Once package PL has been disposed in a secure area of environment or otherwise disposed for secure monitoring e.g. using accessory component by deliverer DL system may continue to intermittently or continuously monitor package PL and or the secure area e.g. area AL to maintain the security of the dropped off package. As one example environment may be configured to continuously or intermittently monitor the position of dropped off package PL such as by detecting status data from accessory component coupled to package PL or by sensing package PL within area AL or by confirming that a secure area e.g. a lobby or safe has remained inaccessible since disposal of package PL therein. After any suitable monitoring period of any suitable length during which the security of package PL has been confirmed by environment system may be configured to communicate such security status with any suitable entity such as delivery entity business and or any suitable user of environment e.g. an intended recipient of package PL . However if at any time after secure disposal of package PL by deliverer DL environment detects any type of change in the status of package PL or of a secure area or component with which environment may be securing package PL any suitable sensing functionality of environment may be activated or enhanced and or any suitable alarm or notification functionality may be activated. For example if any movement of package PL is detected by environment e.g. by a motion sensing component of doorbell additional sensing components of environment e.g. a camera sensor of doorbell and or other helpful components of environment e.g. outdoor lighting may be activated to sense additional information about the status of package PL and or its surroundings e.g. whether an animal or other entity may be moving package PL . Alternatively or additionally in such instances an alarm may be activated and communicated within structure e.g. if any occupancy currently exists within structure and or outside of environment e.g. at doorbell and or to any suitable law enforcement entities or delivery entity business or users of environment for aid in securing package PL . When a package PL has been deposited by deliverer DL for secure monitoring by environment any suitable events may be monitored for enhancing the protection of package DL including for example detecting when any unknown user or visitor may come within a certain distance of a secure area at which package PL has been deposited. For example doorbell or any other suitable portion of smart environment that may be able to monitor package PL may be equipped with walkup identification technology e.g. face recognition RFID ultrasonic sensors that may fingerprint or create or otherwise have access to a signature for known users of environment such that in operation when a person who does not live in the home or is otherwise not registered with the smart home or whose fingerprint or signature is not recognized by the smart home walks up to package PL environment may provide an alarm and or may increase the protection of package PL by activating a new form of package monitoring securing e.g. a more sensitive movement sensor with respect to package PL .

As mentioned when a package PL has been left by a deliverer DL at environment system may be configured to communicate information indicative of that package deposit to any suitable entity e.g. a system user of environment and or delivery entity business and the like . Additionally or alternatively system may be configured to send any suitable reminders at any suitable moment to a system user or delivery entity or other suitable entity that may keep such an entity mindful of the status of a package that has been left at environment but that has not yet been claimed by a system user.
