Such reminders may be achieved via any suitable communication technique such as e mail telephone text message alert via any suitable smart device e.g. via a user interface of a hazard device within structure or via a user interface of doorbell that may be easily identified by a user of environment upon waking up within structure or arriving to door of structure . As just one example when a known system user of environment arrives at structure e.g. at door doorbell may be operative to detect that arrival and responsive thereto communicate to that user that package PL has been recently left by deliverer DL for user retrieval e.g. an audible or textual message via an output component of doorbell that may state welcome home user X a package PL was delivered by delivered by deliverer DL at time Y and is currently secured at location Z awaiting your retrieval . Alternatively a simple blinking light may be provided by doorbell e.g. projector when a package is awaiting user retrieval.

When a previously deposited package PL is awaiting user retrieval e.g. from a secure area being monitored by environment environment may be configured in various suitable ways for enabling secure retrieval of the package. In some embodiments certain particular users may be designated by system as authorized to retrieve a securely monitored package PL. For example an appropriately credentialed system user associated with environment generally and or package PL specifically may be enabled by system to identify one or more particular people that environment may allow to retrieve package PL. In such circumstances facial detection or other suitable fingerprint or signature detection capabilities of a smart device of environment may be leveraged to detect a particular user that system may be configured to determine has been authorized e.g. automatically or by rules based inferencing techniques or by specific user designation etc. to securely retrieve package PL. Alternatively certain entities may be provided with a particular security PIN or other suitable code that may be received by environment e.g. by doorbell and confirmed by system as a trusted pass for securely retrieving package PL. For example if an intended recipient of package PL is a known system user of environment and that user receives a communication e.g. at step that deliverer DL has successfully performed a secure unsupervised drop off of package PL in a secure area of environment that user may interface with system e.g. via personal device in any suitable way for enabling another entity e.g. a neighbor to retrieve that package PL on his or her behalf e.g. that communication received by the user may include a code generated by platform whereby the user may share that code with any entity for use by that entity at environment for re enabling accessibility to the secure area of the smart environment for collecting the disposed package . As one example the user may create a security clearance within system e.g. by sharing the identity of that entity with system such that when the entity is detected at environment e.g. at doorbell environment may be configured to share the location of the secured package PL with the entity and to at least temporarily grant access to that secured area for package retrieval. As another example the user may instruct system to generate a security code that may enable access to the securely monitored package and the user may then share that security code with the entity to retrieve the package e.g. by e mailing or otherwise communicating that code to the entity e.g. via communication techniques of system . As another example system may be operative to define a particular period of time during which the securely monitored package may be accessible for retrieval by any entity. For example a system user may interface with system e.g. via personal device in any suitable way for defining a future time period e.g. between 5 00 and 5 15 pm this afternoon during which system may be operative to alter certain security monitoring techniques that may enable any entity to effectively retrieve the package PL. As just one example although camera monitoring of the secure area at which package PL has been deposited may continue through the defined time period an alarm or other security features may be disabled during that time such that an entity may successfully retrieve the package without triggering any unnecessary enhanced security. Alternatively or additionally automatic deduction may be utilized by system for enabling environment to safely allow retrieval of a monitored package PL when certain situations arise. For example when a known system user is detected by environment within a threshold distance of package PL and then package PL is concurrently moved from the secure area then system may not sound any alarms but may simply allow the package to be retrieved and may communicate confirmation of such retrieval along with any other suitable information e.g. time and date of the retrieval identity of the detected system user associated with that retrieval etc. to any suitable entity e.g. to the recipient user associated with package PL deliverer entity business etc. via any suitable communication capability of system . As another example even if no entity is specifically detected when the package is retrieved if door is legitimately opened within a certain duration of time prior to or after such retrieval then no alarm may be generated and the retrieval may be communicated by system to any appropriate target.

When a package PL is retrieved at environment after being securely monitored system may be configured to obtain any suitable information in order to confirm user receipt of the package and or to otherwise appropriately complete the delivery process of that package. For example depending on any delivery requirements for a particular package as may be determined by system during data detection and or analysis of steps various data may be obtained by system during retrieval of package PL. In some embodiments when package retrieval is enabled any suitable signature or confirmation of receipt action may be collected or otherwise detected by system from the retrieving entity e.g. the intended recipient system user or a neighbor granted retrieval rights as described above . For example environment may instruct the retrieving entity to communicate its identity to environment e.g. via a sensing component or user interface of doorbell or otherwise environment may indicate that an alarm will be sound. As another example environment may require that a retrieving entity present the retrieved package at a suitable smart device of environment or to any other suitable component of system within a suitable period of time after retrieval otherwise environment may indicate that an alarm will be sound. In such embodiments the retrieving entity may position the retrieved package PL in functional view of a sensing component of a smart device of system e.g. position label ID within a sensing area of a sensing component of doorbell or within a sensing area of a sensing component of any other smart device other than doorbell e.g. a hazard device of structure or a personal device or smart environment device of the retrieving entity which may be a user of a neighboring environment that is not environment but that is also a part of system such that system may confirm that package PL has been retrieved at a certain time and or by a certain entity that may be in communication with system . Such sensed information by system may be leveraged by system to achieve a certain amount of trust with respect to the security of the retrieved package such that a confirmation communication may be sent e.g. at an iteration of step to one or more suitable parties e.g. an intended recipient system user and or delivery entity business to confirm successful retrieval of package PL from a securely monitored area of environment thereby enabling closure of that delivery. Such data may be invaluable to a delivery entity that may otherwise never determine if when a package left at a particular location was actually received by a trusted entity.

One some or all of the various sub processes described above with respect to enabling a secure delivery of a package by a deliverer to a system user of environment may provide for enhanced security data to be collected and shared throughout the delivery. For example at any one or more of step e.g. where information related to a package delivery attempt may be detected by environment step e.g. where additional system information related to the delivery may be acquired and analyzed step e.g. where any suitable data may be communicated between system and any suitable system user to further an attempted package delivery step e.g. where any suitable feedback or instructions may be communicated by system to a deliverer of the package or to a potential retriever of the package or any other suitable visitor e.g. at doorbell step e.g. where any suitable action or characteristic of the package or of a deliverer or of any other suitable visitor may be detected during an attempted package delivery and or step e.g. where any suitable confirmation of a detected action may be communicated by system to an entity at environment e.g. at doorbell or to any other suitable entity e.g. a system user and or a delivery entity business during an attempted package delivery of process any suitable data may be collected stored processed or otherwise analyzed by platform e.g. by environment and or system and shared with any suitable entity for enhancing the security and or convenience of an attempted package delivery.

Time stamps specific identification of packages and or visitors e.g. deliverers and retrievers specific actions of packages and or of visitors e.g. deliverers and or of retrievers and the like may be sensed collected stored and shared by environment and or system with any suitable entities such as system users other smart environments trusted third party entities e.g. businesses and any other suitable data targets. Such data collection and sharing may reduce any insurance liability previously held by a delivery entity business that may otherwise have had to attempt delivery of a package multiple times due to an environment being unable to securely receive the package during an initial attempt and or have left a package at an environment in an insecure fashion e.g. on a front stoop of a user without any smart devices of the environment being operative to securely monitor the package until it was appropriately retrieved etc. . As another example such data collection and sharing may enable better tracking of the handling of a package e.g. in order to determine when during the delivery process the package may have been ruined e.g. for fragile package contents where one or more sensors of environment may for example continuously or intermittently monitor and share movement data of a package as the package is deposited at environment by deliverer DL as the package is secured prior to retrieval and or as the package is retrieved. This also may enable accurate location and time tracking of deliverer DL and package PL by detecting and logging data at environment e.g. by enabling deliverer DL to check in to environment and or check out from environment . Moreover rather than relying on delivery information generated and reported by deliverer DL e.g. via data entered into delivery device by deliverer DL during an attempted delivery system may generate and report its own data that may be compared to and or relied on by delivery entity business instead of any data generated by deliverer DL as system data e.g. as may be generated by doorbell may be trustworthy as an impartial data source e.g. as compared to a deliverer who may enter incorrect data to inflate his efficiency and or hide his inefficiencies .

By enabling communication between system and delivery entity business status information about deliverer DL known to delivery entity business may be shared with system whereby system may leverage a known status of environment e.g. modes current future occupancy data current functionality of certain smart devices etc. in combination with the shared status information about deliverer DL to enhance the handling of a potential delivery at environment by deliverer DL. As one example delivery entity business may communicate to system an estimated time of arrival for deliverer DL at environment such that system may communicate with smart environment in order to accommodate the arrival of deliverer DL e.g. by turning on outdoor lighting to enable safe and easy access to door by deliverer DL and or by turning off any sprinkler system smart device not shown that may otherwise impair the deliverer s ability to easily bring package PL to door e.g. to prevent package PL from getting wet . Additionally or alternatively as another example delivery entity business may communicate to system information identifying the deliverer DL in order to improve the ability of environment to detect the expected deliverer e.g. by enhancing certain sensing functionality of one or more smart devices e.g. pre loading a picture of the expected deliverer to increase efficiency of facial detection or turning on additional sensors that may specifically attempt to detect characteristics of the expected visitor etc. . Additionally or alternatively as another example delivery entity business may communicate to system information identifying the contents of package PL e.g. contents requiring a cold environment to stay fresh in order to improve the ability of environment to appropriately receive the expected package e.g. by turning on a cooling feature of a secure area e.g. an air conditioner within the safe area of safe appliance . Such communication may also enhance convenience of the delivery process for a recipient user or any other suitable user of environment as system may be operative to continuously keep that user up to date with respect to the delivery status and security of package PL while enabling that user control over how that package may be delivered deposited and or retrieved. For example in response to system receiving status information from delivery entity business about an upcoming planned delivery to environment system may be operative to analyze that status information e.g. in combination with any current modes or other information associated with environment and may then automatically communicate certain information to a system user about that planned delivery e.g. via any suitable smart device or personal user device such that the system user may update any suitable mode settings or define a new mode or otherwise provide instructions to system for handling the planned delivery once the deliverer and or package are physically detected at environment . Additionally or alternatively by enabling communication between system and delivery entity business status information about environment and or system users associated therewith known to system may be shared with delivery entity business and or deliverer DL. As mentioned above e.g. with respect to a status of environment indicative that environment is in a do not disturb mode for times X Y and Z as may be shared by system with delivery entity business e.g. after status information about deliverer DL known to delivery entity business may be shared with system may enable delivery entity business to more efficiently schedule attempted deliveries to environment e.g. to adjust a planned and or current delivery attempt . As another example a status of environment indicative of the ability of smart environment to securely monitor a package during an unsupervised drop off as may be shared by system with delivery entity business e.g. after status information about deliverer DL known to delivery entity business may be shared with system may enable delivery entity business to more confidently deliver a package to environment even if a do not disturb status of environment may not be known.

Smart doorbell of environment may be configured to include any suitable combination of any of the components described above so as to appropriately interact with other smart devices of environment and services platform and any suitable user thereof such as users registered with or associated with environment e.g. owners occupants etc. and or users visiting environment e.g. package deliverers friends solicitors strangers and would be thieves . In addition to or as an alternative to increasing the convenience and efficiency of package delivery increasing the traceability of package delivery and or enabling secure package delivery such a smart doorbell may be a visitor interface or entryway interface device that may be operative to detect and control or otherwise handle a person s approach to or departure from a location e.g. an outer door of structure of environment announce such an approach or departure enhance conventional doorbell functionality for both residents and visitors control settings on a security system detect environmental data and other useful data for environment and system and the like. Therefore doorbell on behalf of smart environment and system and users associated therewith may act as a security custodian to environment with respect to any visitors that may approach environment where the behavior of such custodial action may be based on any suitable information of system including any suitable modes or settings of any suitable portion or entirety of smart environment and or of a user of such a smart environment.

Any suitable type of mode such as a do not disturb mode may be set for a particular system user U for a particular environment and or for at least a particular portion of a particular environment indefinitely or for any suitable length of time that may start at a current or future moment. Such a mode may be determined based on any suitable information generated by or inferred from any suitable data of environment and or user U available to platform . As just one particular example as mentioned above system may use tracking information to make inferences regarding the current and or future occupancy of home environment and or the current and or future location of a user U e.g. at environment like user UL of and Husband of or away from environment like user UR of and Wife of where such inferences may be used to define a current or future mode of environment and or of a user U. As another example platform may leverage sensed data from one or more sensors of one or more smart devices of environment to at least partially define a particular current or future mode for environment e.g. programs algorithms may assess detected sounds vibrations and movements to determine whether the home occupants are home or away sleeping or awake etc. . Alternatively or additionally a user U may actively select or otherwise at least partially define a particular current or future mode for environment or a system user by manually communicating mode selection data to system e.g. via direct user interaction with a user device and or any suitable smart device of system accessible by the user . Various determinations of various factors may combine to enable a particular mode for a particular system user and or a particular system environment or specific portion thereof e.g. no occupancy within environment lack of user movement within a darkened bedroom etc. and various settings may be enabled or made available during that enabled mode e.g. turn on lights within environment at a certain time of day to mimic occupancy prevent disruptive communication of an attempted delivery at environment to a darkened room thereof etc. .

For example a do not disturb mode for environment generally may indicate that environment may not be willing or able to accept at least certain package deliveries e.g. deliveries requiring a confirmation of receipt user signature by a particular user or any user . Such a mode may be manually set by an appropriate user e.g. a user with appropriate management rights for environment using any suitable device or interaction with any other suitable smart device of environment for any suitable reason such as when the user does not want to greet a visitor e.g. if the user is feeling under the weather or going to sleep or when the user will not be at environment e.g. when the user is going on vacation or leaving a babysitter at home with a child . Alternatively platform may be operative to collect any suitable information from one or more smart devices of environment and may make inferences in order to automatically set a do not disturb mode for environment e.g. based on sensed occupancy data and sensed movement data . When a current mode of environment is set to a do not disturb mode various suitable settings may be applied by system in response to various suitable detected activities. As just one example in response to a visitor e.g. deliverer DL with or without a package PL being detected by doorbell of environment when environment is in a do not disturb mode system may be operative to automatically initiate a particular action such as communicating to the detected visitor e.g. via user interface or audio speaker of doorbell that it is not an appropriate time to visit environment and to come back at a later time. Additionally or alternatively as mentioned above information indicative of when environment may be associated with a do not disturb mode may be a type of current status information that may be shared with or otherwise made accessible to a facilitator entity e.g. a delivery business for increasing the efficiency of package delivery e.g. delaying delivery until after a do not disturb mode is over and or of any other activity that may include a visitor interacting with environment . Such information may be handled with sensitivity so as to not be leveraged for sinister purposes e.g. for a third party to detect when an environment is in a do not disturb mode so as to assume no one is home and attempt a robbery of the premises . For example communication to a detected visitor of such a mode may simply indicate that an occupant of environment is otherwise preoccupied at the moment e.g. on an important telephone call or putting the baby to sleep and does not wish to interact with the detected visitor whether or not there is in fact an occupant currently at environment where such a communication may be automatically updated or selected by system as may be appropriate for a particular time of day e.g. communicate that an occupant is sleeping if after 10 00 pm or that an occupant is in an important meeting if during regular business hours etc. or for a particular visitor e.g. communicate that an occupant is not available when a known visitor is detected or on an important telephone call when an unknown visitor is detected etc. . As another example system may be configured to share information about a do not disturb mode of an environment or any other suitable status information of environment or a user thereof with a third party such as a facilitator of a package delivery only when certain data is accessible to that third party. For example system may only share such status information when a facilitator entity queries system with respect to particular unique package identification information e.g. such information as may be generated at step and linked with a particular ordered package . Certain facilitator entities e.g. Federal Express may be trusted and enabled by platform to interpret such unique package identification information for appropriately querying system about such status information and whereby system may be configured to only share such status information when queried by a trusted entity e.g. when the unique package identification information is leveraged by an entity trusted by system and not just when any entity has access to the recipient and or location data of the ordered package .

Various types of data may be detected and analyzed for potentially affecting a current or future mode of a system user and or at least a portion of a smart environment. For example user location information with respect to the boundaries of environment or a portion thereof e.g. with respect to a particular room of structure may be leveraged for determining a system mode. If no user is detected within a particular room of environment then that room may be put into a do not disturb mode such that no information is fruitlessly attempted to be communicated to an occupant of that room e.g. via any smart devices of that room . As another example if an occupant is detected within a particular room of environment but that occupant is detected to have not moved more than a particular threshold amount in a particular amount of time and or a brightness value of light is below a particular threshold in that room then it may be inferred that the occupant is asleep and that room may be put into a do not disturb mode such that no information is communicated to an occupant of that room e.g. via any smart devices of that room to prevent the occupant from being awoken. Additionally or alternatively any other suitable activity of a user may be detected by one or more smart devices for at least partially determining a mode of the user and or environment . For example platform may determine that a user is conducting a video conference call with business partners e.g. by analyzing certain movements and actions of the user in conjunction with detected operation of one or more appliances or electronic devices of environment e.g. a video conferencing machine or television or user device and may utilize that information to infer that the user should not be bothered during that activity. In certain embodiments calendar data may be accessible and analyzed for determining a system mode. For example a calendar application for a particular user e.g. as may be accessible by a processing component of platform from a user device may be accessed and analyzed e.g. independently or in combination with other detected data to determine a current or future activity of the user e.g. leveraging calendar data indicative of an important telephone call with client X at a current time in combination with detection of the user being on the telephone may be used to enable a do not disturb mode for that user during the duration of that telephone call .

Additionally or alternatively a user may affirmatively provide platform with information that may be leveraged to at least partially determine one or more modes to be enabled. For example a user may communicate any suitable information to platform via any suitable device of environment to define any suitable characteristic that may be analyzed for enabling a mode and or to specifically enable a particular mode. In some embodiments a user may communicate to platform e.g. via a user device and or any suitable user interface of any suitable smart device of environment a particular activity that the user is currently performing or will be performing at a future time such as putting my baby down for a nap or conducting an important business call or reading an important work document or feeling under the weather or the like. Such information may be verbally communicated by the user to platform or may be manually entered by interfacing with a graphical user interface or any other suitable user interface of platform . Such information may be communicated to platform by a user from any suitable location whether or not the user is local to a particular environment for affecting a mode of that environment. For example a user that may have recently left environment via car may utilize its personal device for communicating to platform that the user wishes for a do not disturb mode to be enabled for environment . In some embodiments a particular mode may be set manually by a user e.g. to override any alternative mode that might be enabled based on current detected data such as to enter a do not disturb mode for the entirety of environment despite a child and a babysitter currently actively occupying environment .

Each one of multiple different system users can be associated with its own distinct mode. For example a first user occupant of environment may be in a do not disturb mode e.g. when on an important telephone call or simply when wishing to not be disturbed and a second user occupant of environment may not be in a do not disturb mode whereby platform may be operative to balance the settings of each enabled mode of the various occupants of environment when responding to an event e.g. when a visitor is detected e.g. at step platform may communicate with a personal device associated with the second user e.g. at step while platform may avoid any communication with devices of environment that may disturb the first user . As one example platform may be operative to communicate silently with a user device of a first available user via a smart device that is proximate to a first available user e.g. with silent blinking lights or text message on a user interface of such a smart device but not to communicate in any manner that may disturb a not available user that may be sleeping next to the available user e.g. not with an audible message via a smart device proximate both users . Additionally or alternatively each one of multiple different zones or areas of environment can be associated with its own distinct mode. For example a first room of environment may be in a do not disturb mode e.g. a bedroom when one or more occupants may be resting therein and a second room of environment may not be in a do not disturb mode e.g. a living room where one or more occupants may be casually watching television whereby platform may be operative detect such modes and to balance the settings of each enabled mode of the various rooms of environment when responding to an event e.g. when a visitor is detected e.g. at step platform may communicate with one or more smart devices located within the second room e.g. at step while platform may avoid any communication with any devices of the first room that may disturb the occupant s therein .

Any particular data or combination of various types of data accessible by platform which may be detected or otherwise received by one or more of devices of a smart home environment may be processed by platform e.g. with a processing engine and or services and or third party sources and or paradigms and or extrinsic information and or any other suitable information services for example in combination with rules based inference engines and or artificial intelligence as received home data e.g. for generating derived home data and that data may be analyzed or otherwise used to define and enable a particular mode for a particular user and or for at least a particular portion of an environment . Such a mode may be associated with an entire environment or only a portion thereof. For example a particular wing of structure may be utilized at a certain time as an exhibition area for a performance or a meeting such that that area should be in a do not disturb mode at that time such that information may not be communicated to that area by platform for specific events e.g. for detection of a deliverer DL with a package PL . Additionally or alternatively such a mode may be associated with a particular user whether or not the user is local to environment e.g. user UL or remote from environment e.g. user UR . For example a particular user may be associated with an enabled do not disturb mode when an important business call is being conducted by that user regardless of whether that user is conducting the call within environment or remotely from environment e.g. while driving away from environment such that that user may not be communicated to by platform in a disturbing manner for alerting that user of a specific event e.g. for detection of a deliverer DL with a package PL such as at step .

When a current mode is enabled for a particular environment or user various suitable settings may be followed by platform for that mode in response to particular events being detected. For example when a visitor is detected at environment e.g. at step different type s of communication may be conducted by platform with one or more users depending on whether or not environment is in a particular do not disturb mode e.g. at step and or different type s of feedback may be provided by platform to the visitor depending on whether or not environment is in a particular do not disturb mode e.g. at step . When environment is in a particular type of do not disturb mode for example platform may be operative not to communicate the detection of a visitor using any devices within environment according to communication settings of that mode e.g. so as not to wake any sleeping occupants or so as not to fruitlessly attempt to communicate with non existent occupants yet when environment is not in a do not disturb mode platform may be operative to communicate such detection of a visitor using one or more devices within environment e.g. so as to alert the occupants of the visitor .

In some embodiments certain settings of a particular mode may vary based on certain characteristics of a particular event being detected. For example when a first particular visitor is detected at environment e.g. at step a first particular communication operation may be conducted by platform with a user when environment is in a particular do not disturb mode e.g. at step and or a first particular feedback may be provided by platform to the visitor when environment is in a particular do not disturb mode e.g. at step yet when a second particular visitor is detected at environment e.g. at step a second particular communication operation may be conducted by platform with a user when environment is in that same particular do not disturb mode e.g. at step and or a second particular feedback may be provided by platform to the visitor when environment is in that same particular do not disturb mode e.g. at step . For example when a particular do not disturb mode has been enabled for environment e.g. because the user is taking a nap most visitors detected by environment may be provided by platform with feedback instructing the visitor to return at a later time as the occupants are currently unavailable and no communication may be provided by platform to an occupant that might wake the occupant yet a particular important visitor e.g. a deliverer DL with a highly anticipated or desired package PL detected by environment may be provided by platform with feedback e.g. at step instructing the visitor to wait for an occupant to come to the door and appropriate communication may be provided by platform e.g. at step to the napping occupant e.g. to wake the occupant and instruct the occupant to further the desired delivery process .

Various settings of a particular mode for an environment or system user may dictate the functionality of one or more devices e.g. one or more smart devices of environment . In some embodiments certain mode settings may dictate such functionality in a time based fashion. For example lighting of environment e.g. one or more lamps or outdoor lighting may be automatically turned on 30 minutes before sunset e.g. at 5 00 pm by platform when environment is in a do not disturb mode which may mimic occupant interaction with environment lighting such that environment may appear occupied. Additionally or alternatively in some embodiments certain mode settings may dictate such functionality based on detection of any visitor or a particular visitor. For example lighting of environment e.g. one or more lamps or outdoor lighting may be automatically turned on when a visitor is detected by platform e.g. at doorbell when environment is in a do not disturb mode which may mimic occupant interaction with environment lighting when a visitor is detected such that environment may appear occupied. As another example certain audio e.g. a dog barking may be automatically output e.g. by audio speaker of doorbell when an unknown visitor is detected by platform e.g. at doorbell when environment is in a do not disturb mode which may mimic occupant interaction with environment lighting when a visitor is detected such that environment may appear occupied or otherwise more prepared to thwart a would be thief.

As yet another example certain settings of a mode may dictate that platform automatically provides certain feedback with environment when a particular event is detected while that mode is enabled for environment or a user thereof. For example certain settings of a do not disturb mode may be operative to cause certain feedback e.g. a visual indicator or audible message to be automatically output by environment e.g. by projector user interface and or audio speaker of doorbell when a known visitor or any visitor is detected by platform e.g. by doorbell at environment when such a do not disturb mode is enabled for environment or for a user thereof. Such feedback may be provided e.g. at step to indicate to the visitor detected e.g. at step that no occupant of environment is currently available to interact with the visitor. For example such feedback may convey to the detected visitor that occupant X is currently on an important telephone call right now and cannot be bothered or occupant X is currently nursing the baby please come back at another time or the like which may in some way alert the visitor not to bother interacting any further with environment e.g. not to bother depressing or otherwise interacting with button of doorbell when the visitor is detected such that environment may appear occupied but unable to accommodate occupant interaction with the visitor. As another example such feedback may be provided as a simple indication of the mode on or with respect to user interface doorbell button or any other suitable component of doorbell or other smart device of environment that a visitor would usually interact with to reach an occupant e.g. doorbell button may be provided with a blinking red light or text message reading doorbell deactivated please come back at another time whereby a visitor may easily determine that any active visitor interaction with environment would not be worthwhile. In some such embodiments such feedback may be provided at an initial entry point to environment e.g. at a front gate at the border of the curtilage of environment which may thereby indicate the do not disturb mode to the visitor at an initial detection of the visitor at environment rather than after the visitor has fruitlessly advanced to the front door of structure . This may save valuable time for the visitor e.g. obviating the need for a deliverer DL to get out of a delivery truck with package PL for approaching door and or may prevent more intimate visitor interaction with portions of environment that may disturb an occupant e.g. visitor interaction with front door may needlessly rile up an occupant dog on the interior side of door . In some embodiments in addition to or as an alternative to providing such feedback to a detected visitor certain settings of a do not disturb mode may be operative to adjust certain functionalities of certain devices of environment when a known visitor or any visitor is detected by platform e.g. by doorbell at environment when such a do not disturb mode is enabled for environment or for a user thereof. Such functionality adjustment may include for example deactivating the functionality of platform to communicate an interaction of a visitor with doorbell button to a system user of environment when a particular mode is enabled for environment or a user thereof. That is the conventional functionality of doorbell button may be at least partially deactivated when a particular mode is enabled.

Various levels of detailed information regarding the mode may be communicated in such feedback dependent upon the type of visitor detected. For example if a deliverer DL of a trusted third party deliverer entity is detected e.g. at step then platform may be operative to provide feedback e.g. at step that may indicate when the current do not disturb mode will be over e.g. no one is currently available to receive you but please return between 3 00 pm and 5 00 pm when an occupant will be ready to greet you . However if an unknown visitor is detected then less detailed feedback may be provided such as no one is currently available to receive you please leave the premises immediately . In certain embodiments platform may be configured to provide visitor specific messages to specific visitors that may be detected during specific modes. For example when an occupant is set to take a nap and instructs platform to enable a do not disturb mode for the user and or at least a portion of environment but that occupant wishes to leave a message for a particular visitor if that visitor is detected during that mode e.g. Hi visitor Y I am sorry to miss you but I had to take a nap I left your backpack next to the mailbox for you the occupant may provide specific instructions for associating such a message with that mode and that message may be communicated to such a visitor if that visitor is detected by platform e.g. at doorbell when environment is in such a do not disturb mode. Such messages or other suitable customizable settings of a mode may be defined by a user when local to environment e.g. via any suitable smart device of environment or when remote from environment e.g. via a user device such as for example when the user is currently on vacation but would like to leave a customized note for a visitor that is expected to arrive at environment while the user is still on vacation and environment is in a do not disturb mode .

Certain current mode information and or future mode information of an environment or user may be shared with one or more suitable outside service providers. For example as mentioned above with respect to current status information e.g. mode of an environment or user may be obtained by a delivery facilitator business entity e.g. at step to affect the delivery of a package e.g. to delay delivery until a time when environment may be occupied by the recipient to receive the delivery . As another example current status information e.g. mode of an environment or user may be obtained by a law enforcement agency and or suitable emergency response entity or other suitable security entity or neighboring environment to affect protection of the environment or its users e.g. to increase security from thieves of environment in a do not disturb mode until an active occupant is within environment . Mode status information of a smart system entity may include various types of information that may be obtained and leveraged e.g. at steps by a third party for more efficiently delivering a package and or for protecting an environment entity that may be accomplished in a more convenient manner for environment or for a user thereof. For example such status information may include information indicative of when to allow delivery to a particular location e.g. after 4 00 PM on Mondays and Wednesdays only information indicative of preferred alternate delivery methods e.g. do not deliver to environment but rather hold a particular package at a particular deliverer pick up location for manual pick up by a particular user or deliver to another recipient and or to another location other than the recipient and or location initially defined at step information indicative of authorization to deliver without signed confirmation of receipt of delivery e.g. a particular authenticated user of the system hereby authorizes deliverer to deliver a particular package to a particular location and leave next to the front door of that location without a human user sitting for that delivery and or any other suitable information indicative of any other suitable delivery preferences or delivery instructions. As another example such status information may include information indicative of when an environment is more susceptible to certain security breaches e.g. no occupants will be alert at environment after 11 00 PM on Mondays and at all on Wednesdays information indicative of current occupancy on a room by room basis e.g. one child in room A two adults in room B etc. which may be leveraged for increasing the ability of security personnel to handle a situation e.g. a fire information indicative of last detected movement on a room by room basis e.g. movement detected within room A 10 minutes ago movement detected from room B into room C 5 seconds ago etc. which may be leveraged for increasing the ability of security personnel to handle a situation e.g. a robbery information indicative of authorization to access environment without real time user approval e.g. information indicative of user authorization of a particular authenticated security entity e.g. an authenticated firefighter to access at least certain portions of environment without a human user authorizing such access in real time which may be leveraged for increasing the ability of security personnel to handle a situation e.g. a fire and or any other suitable information indicative of any other suitable security preferences or security instructions.

In some embodiments mode status information may be provided to a delivery facilitator and or a security facilitator on a macro level in addition to or as an alternative to providing mode status information with respect to just one particular environment and or user thereof. For example mode status information may be made available to a facilitator entity that may be generally indicative of a mode status or mode trend of a particular group of smart system entities e.g. a neighborhood or ZIP code that may include multiple smart environments . As just one example such mode status information may be indicative of certain days of the week when a majority of such environments of the group are in a do not disturb mode and or are otherwise not available to receive packages and such information may be leveraged by the facilitator entity to increase security to that entire group e.g. neighborhood of environments during those days and or to avoid scheduling deliveries to that entire group e.g. neighborhood of environments during those days. Any suitable grouping of environments or users or other suitable smart system entities of any suitable size and type may be used to generate group or macro level mode status information that may be made available to a facilitator entity for more efficiently handling the purpose e.g. security and or deliveries associated with that group. By grouping smart system entities and only sharing mode status data at a group level with third parties such as delivery facilitator entities the privacy and or security of certain environments may be protected by platform by not sharing mode status information associated specifically with only a particular single environment or user e.g. to preserve at least some anonymity about the status of a particular smart environment or user .

By accessing certain mode status information of a smart environment or other suitable smart system entity of platform as may be detected or inferred by system a facilitator entity may be configured to optimize package delivery or environment security. For example data indicative of when a particular location may and may not be able to receive a package delivery may be processed by any suitable distribution system to dictate when certain packages are dispatched for maximizing the likelihood of a successful physical delivery. This may reduce overhead costs for a delivery entity e.g. reduce fuel prices and wasted man hours by limiting the number of failed delivery attempts and or may reduce insurance costs by limiting the exposure of perishable contents from unnecessary and degrading delivery effects. As another example data indicative of when a particular location may and may not be actively occupied may be processed by any suitable security system to dictate when certain security measures are dispatched for increasing the security of the environment. This may reduce overhead costs for a security entity e.g. reduce fuel prices and wasted man hours by limiting the number of unnecessary visits by a security officer to a location that is currently actively occupied and or may reduce insurance costs by limiting the exposure of environments to less than secure conditions. For example one some or all of steps and may be at least partially or completely automated using one or more computer systems e.g. computer system and or computer system that may be leveraged by each one of environment system facilitator entity and the like for associating a smart system entity of system with a mode and then sharing certain mode status information of that smart system entity with a deliverer or other entity at any suitable time for positively affecting the delivery of a package or the security of the environment or user. A user of system may actively and manually define certain preferences or instructions to be shared with such a facilitator entity. Alternatively or additionally the delivery of packages and or third party security of a user or environment by a facilitator entity may be based on inferences made by system or other suitable processing component s of platform e.g. at environment or remote therefrom and selectively shared with such a facilitator entity e.g. without any active manual preferences made by a user but instead done transparently to a user .

It is understood that the steps shown in process of are merely illustrative and that existing steps may be modified or omitted additional steps may be added and the order of certain steps may be altered.

Smart doorbell of environment may be configured to include any suitable component or combination of components described above so as to effectively interact with other smart devices of environment and of services platform and with any suitable users thereof such as users registered with or associated with environment e.g. owners occupants etc. and or users visiting environment e.g. package deliverers friends solicitors strangers and would be thieves for increasing the security of environment and or for increasing the convenience of users of environment . For example doorbell may be operative to initially detect a visitor at environment analyze visitor information based on the initial detection e.g. in light of any applicable enabled modes adjust a functionality of one or more smart devices of environment based on such analysis communicate with a user of environment based on such analysis provide feedback to the visitor based on such analysis and or based on such communication detect at least one act performed by the visitor in response to the provided feedback and or communicate with at least one of the user and the visitor based on the detected act. A first adjustment of the functionality of a smart device may be performed based on analysis of initial visitor detection information e.g. based on the detection of a visitor generally while a second adjustment of the functionality of a smart device may be later performed based on analysis of additional visitor detection information e.g. based on the detection of an act of a visitor where detection and analysis of such an act may identify a class of the visitor or that may identify the visitor specifically . Certain adjustment of the functionality of a smart device may enable the visitor to access at least a portion of environment e.g. unlocking of doorknob of door for enabling a visitor to enter structure . Such access may be granted based on analysis of visitor information revealing a trusted invitee e.g. a guest to a party at a specifically designated time or a trusted security service entity e.g. a fireman during a detected emergency situation . The granted access may be limited in one or more ways based on the identity of the visitor and or based on any other suitable data available for analysis. Various additional data may be leveraged during the analysis of any suitable detected visitor information including data from a neighborhood security network of one or more additional smart environments associated e.g. physically with environment . Each one of these various security features that may be provided by doorbell and platform for enhancing visitor handling at environment is described below in more detail.

As described above at step of process for enhancing visitor handling visitor information of a visitor may be detected at an entryway interface device of a smart environment. For example one or more sensing components of doorbell may be operative to detect any suitable visitor information when any suitable visitor comes within a suitable sensing range of doorbell . Such a visitor may be any suitable entity such as a package deliverer e.g. deliverer DL of which may be a human or a drone or otherwise security entities e.g. firemen policemen security system agents etc. any other suitable agents of any third party entities known to platform e.g. entities friends of one or more users of environment that may or may not be known to platform solicitors strangers would be thieves and the like. At step first visitor identification information may be detected when a visitor is initially sensed by platform at environment e.g. by doorbell . Such initial first visitor identification information may be any suitable detectable data that may then be analyzed by platform e.g. at step in order to determine that a visitor may be present at environment . For example simple motion data e.g. as may be sensed by a motion sensing component of doorbell may be adequate for analysis by platform e.g. by doorbell alone in combination with other processing components of environment and or in combination with other processing components of platform such as system to determine that a visitor is present at doorbell . Alternatively more advanced sensing may be performed at step for initially detecting the presence of a visitor at step e.g. motion sensing audio sensing camera sensing PIR sensing ambient light sensing ultrasonic sensing and or any other suitable sensing capabilities of doorbell or of environment generally e.g. sensing capabilities of one or more other smart devices . As just one example audio sensing of a fingerprint or signature matching a delivery truck or any other suitable vehicle that may be generally associated with a visitor may be initially detected and analyzed which may result in additional visitor sensing functionality being enhanced for further detection and analysis e.g. video sensing and or motion sensing .

At step process may include analyzing the detected visitor information of step e.g. in conjunction with any other suitable data available to platform such as settings of a current mode of environment or of a user for determining the presence of a visitor at environment and how to initially respond to such a determination. For example in response to detecting such visitor information at step doorbell alone or in combination with other processing components of other smart devices and or rules based inference engines and or artificial intelligence provided locally at environment and or at or in conjunction with system and or at or in conjunction with any other component s of services platform may be operative at step to access any suitable additional information that may be useful for interpreting the detected visitor information e.g. motion sensing thresholds visitor signatures or fingerprints and or any other suitable data that may help to make a determination about the presence of a visitor in light of the detected visitor information and or additional information that may be useful for determining how to proceed if the presence of a visitor is determined e.g. current mode settings of environment etc. and then to analyze all such available information for determining whether or not a visitor is present and if so whether to take one or more of a variety of automated actions based on that detected visitor presence.

At step process may include adjusting the functionality of at least one smart device of environment based on the analysis of step or even based solely on the detection of step . As just one example when any potential visitor information is detected at step smart environment may be operative to turn on a light e.g. outdoor lighting or projector of doorbell at step to increase the safety of the potential visitor and or to increase the security of environment . As another example when any potential visitor information is detected at step smart environment may be operative to increase the sensing functionality of one or more smart devices of environment at step e.g. by increasing the sampling rate of a sensing component by increasing or varying the sensing area covered by a sensing component by turning on one or more additional sensing components e.g. of doorbell that may have previously been turned off for power conservancy etc. to increase the security of environment e.g. by enhancing the ability of environment to monitor any potential visitor activity . As another example when any potential visitor information is detected at step smart environment may be operative to generate certain activity at step that may mimic occupancy at environment detectable by the visitor to increase the security of environment such as by turning on a lamp within structure and or by outputting audio data from an audio output component of any smart device within structure that may resemble a dog barking or any other suitable noises or activity that may lead a visitor to believe that an active occupant is at environment . In some embodiments such audio data may be output by an audio output component of a device located within structure but adjacent to door such that the outputted audio e.g. a played back recording of a dog barking may realistically sound like occupancy within structure . In other embodiments such as when an actual dog is known to be within structure audio data that is only audible to a dog may be output by an audio output component of environment which may prompt the actual dog to bark for increasing the security of environment . As yet another example when any potential visitor information is detected at step smart environment may be operative to output a general message at step that may instruct the visitor how to initially interface with environment e.g. by outputting audio data from audio speaker or visual data from projector of doorbell or any other suitable data from any other suitable smart device of environment that may be received by the detected visitor where such a message may include any suitable instruction such as Please identify yourself and your intention or Please align any identification information with a sensing component of the doorbell or the like to increase the security of environment and further the visitor handling of process . As another example when any potential visitor information is detected at step smart environment may be operative to lock any unlocked entry ways to structure e.g. by locking smart doorknob at step to increase the security of environment whereby in such embodiments the previous locked unlocked condition of such entry ways may be restored once the visitor is no longer detected or has been otherwise securely dealt with.

Such adjusting of the functionality of one or more smart devices of environment at step may be based on the analysis of step . For example such adjusting may be done automatically in response to a determination that the presence of a visitor has been detected. Additionally or alternatively such adjusting may be done automatically not only in response to a determination that the presence of a visitor has been detected but also in response to analysis of any applicable mode settings rules inferences or other suitable information available to platform that may be processed for determining the way or ways in which certain smart device functionality ought to be adjusted in response to the determined visitor presence e.g. time of day current functionality of certain smart devices current mode of environment current occupancy of environment and or any other suitable information . Such adjusting may also be performed whether or not the detected visitor presence has been determined with respect to a particular visitor e.g. next door neighbor John Doe with respect to a particular visitor type e.g. a delivery drone or a gas utility service man or security agent or firefighter etc. or with respect to a visitor generally e.g. a human or drone or any other suitable entity that may be handled by platform as a potential visitor to environment even including an animal such as a cat that may be detectable as an unknown stray or detectable as the neighbor s missing pet e.g. via an NFC chip coupled to the cat and NFC sensing component whereby process may enable proper detection of the cat and communication of its presence to appropriate users authorities . Such initial detection of the presence of a visitor may be determined based on analysis of initial detected visitor information that may be compiled without active communication by the visitor of its intent to environment . Instead in some embodiments the presence may be initially determined when the analysis of the visitor information determines that the shape and or motion and or any other suitable characteristic of a potential visitor e.g. generically or specifically has been detected. Such initial adjusting of the functionality of one or more smart devices at step in response to initial detection of the presence of a visitor may automatically increase the security of environment and or increase the safety or convenience of the detected visitor that may be potentially attempting to interact with environment for any suitable purpose e.g. for communicating with an occupant for delivering a package for fetching an item etc. .

It is understood that the steps shown in process of are merely illustrative and that existing steps may be modified or omitted additional steps may be added and the order of certain steps may be altered.

As described above at step process may include communicating with a user associated with the smart environment based on the analysis of step . As just one example when the analysis of step determines that the presence of a visitor has been initially detected at environment and that a mode of environment or of a system user is such that communication may be attempted smart environment may be operative to communicate the determined visitor presence to an appropriate system user or portion of environment in any suitable way at step e.g. by audibly announcing any suitable information related to the visitor presence via an audio speaker of a smart device that may be located most proximal to the current location of a user within environment . As another example when the analysis of step determines that no appropriate user is available within environment smart environment may be operative to communicate the visitor presence to a system user or appropriate third party via platform in any suitable way at step e.g. by transmitting an electronic message to a personal device associated with a remote user UR or by transmitting an electronic message to a trusted third party security entity associated with environment . For example in some embodiments a video e.g. a recorded loop or a live stream of the detected visitor or still image or any other suitable detected visitor information e.g. as detected at step may be communicated at step to such a user or third party automatically or in response to a request relayed from such a user or third party after being notified of the detected visitor whereby such communicated visitor information data may be utilized by such a user or third party in any suitable way e.g. to actively monitor the visitor s activity and or to attempt to specifically identify the identity of the visitor or at least the type of the identified visitor .

At step process may include providing the visitor with feedback based on at least one of the analysis of step and or any communication of step . As just one example when the analysis of step determines that there are currently no occupants local to environment or otherwise in an active and available state for appropriately being told of the detected visitor and or when no user response is received for any communication attempt of step with respect to a detected visitor platform may be operative to determine that smart environment may proceed with handling the detected visitor without active user input and doorbell may provide the visitor at step with instructions or other suitable feedback on how to proceed. Alternatively when the analysis of step determines that there is a user local to environment that is in an active and available state for appropriately being told of the detected visitor and or when a user or third party response is received for any communication attempt of step with respect to a detected visitor platform may be operative to determine that a user or third party privy to smart environment may at least partially handle the visitor and doorbell may provide the visitor at step with instructions or other suitable feedback on how to proceed. The type of feedback that may be provided via doorbell and or via any other suitable smart device of environment to the visitor at step may vary based on the analysis of step and or any communication of step . For example the feedback may include active communication from the user or third party to the visitor via doorbell e.g. audible and or visual information and or any other suitable information may be conveyed to the visitor by doorbell where such information may be generated and transmitted by or otherwise under the control of the user via another smart device that the user may directly interface with and that may be communicatively coupled to doorbell . This may enable a virtual conversation between the user and the visitor via platform e.g. by repeating one or more of steps as described above with respect to a deliverer visitor . Alternatively the feedback may include automated messages or instructions generated by system for communication to the visitor via doorbell e.g. a message that may communicate that a user is not currently able to actively interact with you right now please proceed as follows . . . etc. . Additionally or alternatively the feedback may include providing certain environment access to the visitor such as by opening door by unlocking doorknob for a certain amount of time e.g. if the visitor is approved by system as an expected and or authorized visitor door may be unlocked such that the visitor may be enabled to enter structure .

In some embodiments feedback provided by platform at step to an initially detected visitor may convey a request for the detected visitor to provide more and or specific information about the visitor s identity and or the visitor s intent using any suitable output component of doorbell or any other smart device of environment that may be detected by the visitor. For example such feedback may include any suitable audible and or visual request for the visitor to physically communicate with environment such as a request to please state your full name and your intent . As another example such feedback may include any suitable request for the visitor to avail at least a specific portion of the visitor to environment for being properly sensed by environment e.g. within a detection range of a sensing component of doorbell such as a request to please align your face with the doorbell s camera or please present a form of identification to the doorbell s scanner or any other suitable instructions for facilitating the detection of any specific visitor identification information and or visitor intent information. Label ID may be any suitable form of visitor identification such as a label of package PL or a driver s license of the visitor or an identification tag of a delivery drone or an RFID tag of a pet or personal property etc. that may be properly sensed by environment .

At step process may include detecting an act of the visitor based on the provided feedback of step e.g. an act performed by the visitor in response to the provided feedback . Doorbell and or any other smart device of environment may be configured to detect an action of the visitor at step in response to platform providing the visitor with feedback at step where that action may be any suitable action indicative of the visitor interacting with environment e.g. doorbell in a particular way. As just one example in response to instructing the visitor to provide specific information about its identity and or its intent or otherwise to avail at least a specific portion of the visitor e.g. its face or a label ID to sensing by environment for detection of such specific identification information e.g. within a detection range of a sensing component of doorbell at step doorbell may detect such additional visitor identification intent information at step . Any suitable action of the visitor may be detected or otherwise received by any suitable component of environment and or otherwise of platform at step where such detection may enable platform to update system information about the detected visitor such as with respect to the specific identity of the visitor e.g. neighbor Billy Bob the specific type of visitor e.g. Federal Express deliverer child firefighter the specific intent of the visitor e.g. visitor wants to say hi to occupant X visitor wants to deliver package PL visitor wants to pick up an item it accidently left at environment etc. and or the like. For example a visitor may communicate with platform at step via any suitable communication enabled by a smart device of environment accessible by the visitor and or via any suitable communication enabled by platform and a visitor device . In some embodiments suitable visitor identification data may be communicated with platform by the visitor at step via visitor gestures towards doorbell as may be described above with respect to smart device via visitor touch input via a touch user interface via visitor audible spoken information via microphone and or the like. A visitor may scan a driver s license or other suitable identification such as the visitor s face or fingerprint e.g. at a scanner sensing component of doorbell . Additionally or alternatively platform may be configured to automatically detect such additional visitor identification intent information at step without prompting the visitor to do so at step . For example label ID may be automatically detected by a sensing component of doorbell when a visitor is present within a specific distance of doorbell and not in response to a specific act of the visitor done in response to a specific feedback request of platform .

Specific visitor identification intent information detected e.g. at step or initially at step may then be analyzed by platform for more specifically identifying the visitor or its intent e.g. by repeating step . For example platform may be operative to analyze such detected visitor information by running any suitable facial detection or fingerprint or other biometric sensing algorithms or any other suitable entity identification algorithms or comparisons using any available databases or processing paradigms or extrinsic information such as social network contact information of various entities known by the various occupants of environment or known agent information of various business emergency response entities or known sex offenders or criminals or missing person pet identification databases of law enforcement agencies in order to detect or confirm the identity of the visitor. One or more iterations of detecting visitor information analyzing detected visitor information providing the visitor with feedback and or detecting an act of the visitor of process may be conducted by platform e.g. via doorbell any other smart devices of environment and or any other processing capabilities of platform with or without any active communication from a system user or third party in order to determine the identity and or intent of a detected visitor with any suitable amount of clarity confidence accuracy and or specificity for effectively handling the visitor.

At step process may include communicating with at least one of the user and the visitor based on the detected identity and or intent of the visitor. Doorbell and or any other smart device of environment may be configured to confirm detection of an identity and or intent of the visitor with the visitor e.g. by communicating any suitable confirmation information directly to the visitor via doorbell . Alternatively or additionally doorbell and or any other component of environment and or system may be configured to confirm detection of an identity and or intent of the visitor with a user of environment e.g. by communicating any suitable confirmation information to the user via any suitable smart device of environment or personal device of the user similarly to any communication of step . This may enable the visitor and or the user to remain updated with respect to the current status of the handling of the visitor by platform .

One or more of steps of process may be repeated for any suitable visitor handling. For example in response to analysis at step of any visitor information detected at step feedback requesting additional visitor identification information may be provided to the visitor at step in response to which an action of the visitor attempting to provide additional visitor information may be detected by the smart environment at step and any additional visitor information of that detected action may be analyzed at step in response to which one or more of steps may again follow. Therefore process may support a virtual interaction between a visitor and platform e.g. environment or service as an automated agent of a system user .

It is understood that the steps shown in process of are merely illustrative and that existing steps may be modified or omitted additional steps may be added and the order of certain steps may be altered.

Platform may be operative to enable certain functionality of doorbell to being utilized by a visitor whether or not certain visitor identification information and or certain visitor intent information has been confirmed. For example platform may be operative to enable the visitor to leave any suitable message for a system user of environment for eventual receipt by that user e.g. an audio message a video message a text message etc. that may be obtained by one or more sensing components of doorbell . The visitor may simply wish to leave a voicemail message for environment and doorbell may be operative to enable the visitor to record such a message e.g. via microphone whereby such a message may then be eventually communicated to a system user of environment e.g. according to any applicable rules or inferences or mode settings . For example at step doorbell may be operative to provide feedback to the visitor indicative of the ability of doorbell to receive such a message e.g. via audio speaker or projector communicating such a possibility to the visitor such as by conveying a message like leave a voicemail for a user of environment by pressing button now and in response the visitor may communicate such a message to doorbell at step . This may encourage certain types of visitors to interact with environment in a manner that may not unnecessarily bother a user of environment whether or not a do not disturb mode Is enabled for environment or that user. For example a neighbor visitor may be swinging by environment to return a mitten that was accidently left by a system user at the neighbor s home and such a visitor may simply provide a message for capture by platform at step e.g. Hi this is neighbor Billy Bob I am leaving your mitten at your doorstep and platform may then share that message with a system user at a time convenient to the user at step .

Platform may be operative to prevent certain functionality of doorbell from being utilized by a visitor until certain visitor identification information and or certain visitor intent information has been confirmed. For example user interface button of doorbell may be disabled or presented to the visitor as non functional e.g. by displaying a disabled message on the button until any suitable condition has been confirmed by platform . By seemingly presenting the visitor with no ability to ring the bell to beckon an occupant doorbell may encourage a visitor to interact with platform in a cooperative manner e.g. to provide appropriate visitor information at step . This may dissuade a visitor from incessantly pressing button or otherwise interacting with doorbell in an unproductive manner. In such embodiments the actual functionality of doorbell button may be enabled or disabled based on any suitable settings of platform e.g. if a visitor presses doorbell button despite being presented to the visitor as non functional such a visitor interaction may be detected by platform and handled in any suitable way such as by outputting an audible tone at one or more smart devices of environment for alerting an occupant of the visitor and or by storing data indicative of that visitor interaction for later use e.g. for security profiling and or user review as described below .

When platform may attempt to analyze certain system data e.g. at step and or to communicate with a system user during process e.g. at step such as for enabling a user to decide actively how platform may proceed with handling a detected visitor platform may also be operative to simultaneously communicate certain information to the detected visitor while such analysis and or user communication is attempted. For example certain feedback may be provided by environment e.g. by doorbell to a detected visitor at step while platform may also be at least attempting to analyze data at step and or to communicate with a user at step . Such feedback may be provided for maintaining the visitor s attention and or for providing security to environment . As one example such feedback may be a communication instructing the visitor to wait for further instructions e.g. by playing hold music or hold video e.g. an advertisement or telling the visitor please wait a moment which may maintain the visitor s attention and or ensure the visitor that their arrival is being handled. Any other suitable message which may be customizable by a system user and utilized by platform based on current mode settings or otherwise may be provided to a detected visitor e.g. if you are a solicitor please leave this property immediately otherwise you are hereby agreeing to pay the system user 50 . As another example such feedback may be a communication that may convey to the visitor that some active occupancy exists at environment e.g. by outputting audio of a dog barking from within structure as also described above with respect to step which may increase the security of environment rather than having the visitor wait for instructions amidst silence that may lead the visitor to assume that no one is home whether or not that assumption is correct. The type of such feedback may vary based on the identity and or intent of the visitor as may be already determined by platform .
