This may enable a deliverer with a particular smart invitation e.g. a package label ID containing unique invitation identification information to drop off a package in a lobby of a building without platform granting that deliverer access to any particular residence of that building thereby maintaining certain security of that residence while also providing certain security for that package e.g. that the package is held within a secure area of environment not accessible to untrusted entities e.g. members of the general public that are not able to access that lobby . Such limited accessibility may satisfy certain delivery requirements of a deliverer business entity e.g. drop off requirements generally or even signed recipient receipt requirements if that lobby is deemed secure enough e.g. a lobby of a single residence home to which no non system trusted entities may have accessibility . As another example a platform action associated with a particular smart invitation may enable temporary accessibility to a smart safe e.g. a smart appliance that may be provided by environment adjacent doorbell external to structure e.g. smart appliance the interior of which may be selectively and temporarily made accessible to deliverer DL e.g. via any suitable control signals of system by platform for enabling placement of package PL therein in response to detection of the smart invitation e.g. package label ID at doorbell . Any such secure area e.g. a lobby a safe etc. of environment that may be made temporarily accessible to an invitee visitor e.g. deliverer DL by platform e.g. automatically through system processing and control of mode settings of a smart invitation in response to presentation and detection of that smart invitation may be securely monitored by system during such temporary access in order to ensure that deliverer DL positions package PL in that area and or to ensure that nothing is removed from that area during the period of that temporary access. One or more sensing components of doorbell or of any other smart device of environment may be configured to at least partially carry out such monitoring. Additionally or alternatively one or more output components of doorbell or of any other smart device of environment may be configured to at least partially indicate to deliverer DL where and how to deposit the package securely.

A platform action of a mode setting associated with a particular smart invitation for a particular smart environment may be at least partially defined by one or more characteristics defining the details of the smart invitation. For example if a smart invitation is generated in response to an order being placed for delivery of contents e.g. whereby the unique invitation identification information of the invitation may be based on a confirmation number of that order or otherwise generated based on that order certain information detailing that order e.g. a description of the contents the time the order was placed the intended recipient of the order the facilitator of the order etc. may be automatically associated with the mode setting of that smart invitation e.g. through information sharing from an order facilitator business and system via an API . For example such information may be automatically leveraged by platform for defining certain characteristics of certain platform actions of the mode setting such as a platform action to convey a particular message to occupant s of environment e.g. via any all suitable smart devices of environment such as only those in rooms currently occupied within structure when the smart invitation is detected at environment e.g. at doorbell for example where such a message may convey The delivery of the food order placed at restaurant X by occupant Y at time Z is currently being attempted at door . Therefore not only may a smart invitation be automatically made accessible to the facilitator of an order at the time the order is placed e.g. as may be provided by system to the facilitator or generated by the facilitator and shared with system but one or more suitable platform actions of a mode setting associated with that smart invitation may be at least partially automatically defined by platform based on information associated with that order. This may increase the efficiency with which environment may handle an invitee visitor in response to that visitor presenting a specific smart invitation at environment e.g. if there are multiple people at environment that may have made different food orders and that are currently awaiting the delivery thereof . This may not only increase the convenience of the occupant users by being informed what delivery attempt is currently being detected but this may also increase the convenience of the deliverer by not having to manually announce the particulars of the attempted delivery e.g. Hello this is a delivery for occupant Y by restaurant X but instead by only having to present its smart invitation e.g. a delivery receipt containing the confirmation number i.e. the unique invitation identification information such as of a label ID to environment e.g. doorbell for automatic detection analysis handling by platform .

Smart invitations may be useful to a system user when managing accessibility to environment during times when that system user may not be present at environment . For example when a smart invitation is generated to provide environment accessibility to a somewhat trusted entity e.g. a temporary tenant as may be prevalent in the popular home sharing swapping context a system user may wish to provide certain constraints on the use of the environment by that entity. As just one example total occupancy conditions for such a smart invitation mode setting may be useful to prevent a temporary tenant from hosting large gatherings at environment . If detected occupancy within structure is equal to a certain number a mode setting may prevent additional access to structure through use of a smart invitation. In some embodiments a system user may define a do not disturb mode for environment when environment has been made temporarily accessible to entities that have only limited trust such that deliveries or other types of visitor handling may be suspended or handled in a special way when a temporary tenant has accessibility rights thereby preventing platform from enabling a temporary tenant to receive a package from a deliverer. As mentioned various platform actions may be edited for a smart invitation at any moment by an authorized system user such that a temporary tenant s rights with respect to environment may be varied remotely e.g. by a remote system user UR via system when a situation warrants. For example a system user may be notified by platform that a package has been left within a safe and that system user may then choose to grant temporary accessibility rights to safe to a temporary tenant that may currently have accessibility rights to certain areas of environment but not to safe via a particular smart invitation by editing a mode setting of that smart invitation to now allow accessibility to that safe via use of that smart invitation e.g. if the system user wishes for the package to be moved by the temporary tenant to a cooler climate e.g. a refrigerator .

A smart invitation may be leveraged in any suitable context for increasing the security of environment . For example particular unique invitation identification information of a smart invitation may be associated with a particular security entity e.g. an emergency response entity and a mode setting for that smart invitation may be managed for defining the various ways in which that smart invitation may be used by that security entity for interacting with environment . As just one example a fire department may have access to a particular smart invitation with particular unique invitation identification information that may be associated with a mode setting for environment such that a system user may edit that mode setting for varying the accessibility rights that the fire department may have with respect to environment . In some embodiments such a mode setting may be defined to instruct platform to enable the fire department to access all portions of environment at any time the smart invitation of the fire department is detected by environment e.g. if a system user occupant of environment is elderly and implicitly trusts the fire department in all situations at all times . Alternatively such a mode setting may be defined to instruct platform to enable the fire department to access environment only if no active occupants are detected at environment and a specific hazard is detected at environment when the smart invitation of the fire department is detected by environment e.g. if a system user wishes to allow the fire department to enter environment if no one is home or if everyone is sleeping motionless and at least one smart hazard detector or other smart device of environment detects smoke . Additionally or alternatively to determining physical accessibility to environment as a platform action e.g. via unlocking door with smart doorknob such a mode setting may be defined to instruct platform to convey certain information to the fire department when the smart invitation of the fire department is detected by environment as a platform action e.g. via any suitable output component of doorbell such as the current occupancy of environment and or the specific location of each occupant within environment and or a map of environment and or a listing of hazards detected by various hazard detectors of environment such that the fire department may be adequately informed when handling a potential emergency event at environment . Different conditions may be associated with different platform actions of a particular mode setting of a particular smart invitation. For example when a fire department smart invitation is detected at environment a mode setting may instruct platform to enable access through door only if a particular hazard has been detected by environment and no occupancy motion has been detected by environment whereas that same mode setting may instruct platform to convey detected occupancy status information and or environment map information and or detected hazard information of environment with the fire department visitor e.g. via doorbell at all times or only when no current occupancy is detected.

In some embodiments the particular unique invitation identification information of such a smart invitation available to the fire department may be generated by the fire department and shared with any appropriate component s of platform e.g. system for enabling a mode setting to be defined for that particular unique invitation identification information with respect to various particular smart environments. Therefore the same particular unique invitation identification information of a smart invitation available to the fire department may be used by multiple different system users of platform for defining multiple different mode settings for multiple different smart environments that are to be associated with that particular unique invitation identification information of the fire department which may enable the fire department to use only a single smart invitation with that same particular unique invitation identification information at every smart environment the fire department may potentially visit. This may obviate the need for the fire department to carry around multiple types of skeleton keys or otherwise worry about having to interact with various smart environments in different ways but instead may enable the fire department to present the same smart invitation with the same particular unique invitation identification information at every smart environment and the mode settings for that smart invitation with respect to any particular smart environment may vary based on the desires of the system user of that smart environment. Therefore a system user may be provided with the ability to control and edit the various ways in which platform may handle a fire department when the presence of the fire department is authenticated at environment while the fire department may only need one smart invitation for use with multiple smart environments. The same may be true for any other suitable entity such as a package delivery entity e.g. Federal Express or the local U.S. Postal Service that may have access to a single smart invitation that may be presented at each smart environment e.g. within a particular delivery area covered by that entity and different system users of different environments may define different mode settings for handling that smart invitation. For example a particular entity may be responsible for e.g. provide service to the entirety of the locations within a ZIP Code and the particular entity may share the particular unique invitation identification information of its smart invitation as well as its responsible ZIP Code with platform e.g. with system via API and platform may be operative to define a distinct mode setting based on the particular unique invitation identification information of that smart invitation with each smart environment within that ZIP Code.

It is understood that the steps shown in process of are merely illustrative and that existing steps may be modified or omitted additional steps may be added and the order of certain steps may be altered.

It is understood that the steps shown in process of are merely illustrative and that existing steps may be modified or omitted additional steps may be added and the order of certain steps may be altered.

If handling of a detected visitor at environment enables an attempt to communicate with a system user of environment platform may be operative to provide different feedback to the visitor e.g. at doorbell and to the system user e.g. via a user device or any other suitable smart device of environment proximate the user . Enabling different feedback to be provided to a system user and to a detected visitor may independently enhance the experience of the user and visitor in various ways.

Any suitable handling of the detection of any suitable visitor or invitation at environment may include any suitable communication attempt to a system user associated with environment . For example after initial detection of any visitor generally e.g. at steps and or after detecting a specific act of a visitor e.g. at step platform may be operative to attempt to communicate any suitable information indicative of that detection to a system user e.g. at step and or step whether or not that system user is local to environment e.g. user UL via communication at a personal device of the user and or via communication at any suitable smart device of environment or remote from environment e.g. user UR via communication at a personal device of the user . The content of such a communication to a system user and the manner in which such a communication may be attempted by platform may vary based on any suitable data available to platform such as any suitable information relating to the identification and or intent of the detected visitor the intended user the visitor is attempting to communicate with any mode setting of environment the occupancy status of environment information provided by any third party entity e.g. one or more of entities paradigms and the like. In certain situations the content and or manner of a communication to a system user may vary as more time elapses without receiving a user response.

For example when a particular system user is identified as a target of the communication platform may first attempt to communicate e.g. at step and or step just with that particular system user e.g. by communicating with a personal user device associated with that specific user and or with one or smart devices determined to be local to that specific user e.g. hazard device proximate user UL . However if no user response or other suitable indication is received by platform suggesting that the communication was received by the user e.g. within a particular amount of time or after a particular amount of attempts platform may be operative to adjust the communication attempt by varying a characteristic of the output component s with which a smart device may attempt to facilitate the communication e.g. by increasing the volume of an audibly conveyed message and or by switching to or also using a visual output component e.g. a flickering light of the smart device and or by communicating with additional smart devices e.g. by communicating with additional or all suitable smart devices of environment e.g. with any hazard detectors of environment not specifically associated with a do not disturb mode e.g. not in a sleeping baby s room or all hazard detectors of environment or all smart devices of environment and or by changing the message of the communication attempt e.g. from User UR there is someone at the door for you to Occupants there is someone at the door . Therefore platform may be operative to target one or more specific devices associated with one or more specific users and or one or more specific areas of environment with an initial output characteristic when initially attempting to communicate with a user before expanding that communication attempt to other output characteristics and or other devices and or other environment areas which may limit the amount that such an attempted communication may disturb environment while also maximizing the likelihood of eventually contacting an appropriate occupant. Additionally or alternatively platform may be operative to craft a targeted message for one or more specific users when initially attempting to communicate with a user before expanding the breadth of that message to incite a response from other users which may limit the amount that such an attempted communication may disturb environment while also maximizing the likelihood of eventually contacting an appropriate occupant. After an initial attempt an additional attempt may not only include the use of additional output characteristics or devices or messages but may also continue to employ the characteristics of the initial attempt. Alternatively after an initial attempt an additional attempt may only include the use of additional output characteristics or devices or messages but may not continue to employ the characteristics of the initial attempt e.g. to discontinue a potential disturbance to a user who is unable or unwilling to respond to the initial attempt .

It is understood that the steps shown in process of are merely illustrative and that existing steps may be modified or omitted additional steps may be added and the order of certain steps may be altered.

If handling of a detected visitor by platform enables a visitor to interact with environment e.g. doorbell for actively attempting to communicate with a system user of environment e.g. at step platform may be operative to provide different feedback to the visitor e.g. at doorbell and to the system user e.g. via a user device or any other suitable smart device of environment proximate the user . For example at any suitable time a visitor may actively interact with e.g. depress a doorbell button or other suitable doorbell user interface of doorbell for attempting to communicate with a system user of environment e.g. whether or not such interface may be indicative of being enabled or disabled for such use platform may be operative to communicate information indicative of that visitor interaction with a system user in any suitable manner. In some embodiments such communication to a system user may be based on an adjusted version of that visitor interaction such that certain characteristics of that visitor interaction may be filtered or otherwise processed in order to limit the annoyance of such a communication to the system user and or to otherwise make such a communication as effective as possible.

Platform may be operative to communicate any number of visitor interactions within a certain period of time as a single communication type to a system user. For example if a visitor presses doorbell button ten times within a single ten second period of time or only one time within a single ten second period platform may be operative to generate the same communication for a system user e.g. a single buzzer sound emitted from one or more smart devices within environment and or a single message conveyed within environment e.g. a visitor has rung the doorbell rather than doing so ten times . This may limit the disturbance caused to any system user by platform when communicating such a visitor interaction.

Additionally or alternatively platform may be operative to communicate any length of a visitor interaction within a certain period of time as a single communication type to a system user. For example if a visitor presses and then holds doorbell button for ten seconds straight within a single ten second period of time or presses and then holds doorbell button for only one second within a single ten second period platform may be operative to generate the same communication for a system user e.g. a single buzzer sound emitted for a single second length of time from one or more smart devices within environment rather than doing so for a ten second length of time . This may limit the disturbance caused to any system user by platform when communicating such a visitor interaction.

Platform may be configured in any suitable way e.g. by a system user or automatically through heuristics or rules or inferences or any other suitable data or controlling entity of platform to define the period of time within which one or more visitor interactions may result in a single communication to a system user and or the length of time during which a single visitor interaction may last that may result in a single communication to a system user. This may enable various modes whereby a certain type of visitor interaction may result in different communications to a system user depending on various factors e.g. environment mode occupancy status visitor identification etc. and or user customized settings for how defining particular visitor interaction types may be handled and communicated to that user . In some embodiments a pattern of two or more visitor interactions and or a single interaction of at least a specific length may result in a particular type of communication to a system user. For example if more than a certain amount of visitor interactions are detected within a particular amount of time and or if a single visitor interaction is held for more than a certain amount of time and or any other suitable type of visitor interaction is detected e.g. a specific pattern of multiple visitor interactions of specific types platform may be operative to communicate a respective particular type of alert to a system user e.g. to indicate an urgent visitor disposition or a unique visitor interaction e.g. a specific 7 note shave and a haircut two bits rhythmic interaction by a visitor with a smart device input component may be detected and operative to generate a melodic version of that same shave and a haircut two bits riff as a communication to a system user via a smart device output component . This may enable a certain type of visitor interaction to override certain standard response settings of platform so as to enable a visitor to communicate to a system user an urgent communication or an otherwise unique communication. Therefore while ten visitor depressions of doorbell button within ten seconds may result in the same user communication attempt as one visitor depression within ten seconds e.g. a single buzzer sound emitted from one or more smart devices within environment and or a single message conveyed within environment e.g. a visitor has rung the doorbell so as to not annoy or otherwise disturb a system user by providing ten distinct user communication attempts e.g. ten distinct buzzer sounds eleven visitor depressions of doorbell button within ten seconds may result in a different e.g. more urgent user communication attempt e.g. multiple buzzer sounds emitted from one or more smart devices within environment and or a single but stronger message conveyed within environment e.g. a visitor has URGENTLY rung the doorbell . Therefore while platform may be operative to filter down certain annoying visitor interaction types for providing a more palatable alert to a system user platform may also be operative to determine certain visitor interaction types to be urgent or otherwise unique in nature for providing a more urgent or otherwise unique alert to a system user. While visitor interactions with environment have been described with respect to visitor depressions or other suitable interactions with a doorbell button which may be similar to some conventional visitor interactions with conventional doorbells intercoms e.g. for ringing a doorbell any suitable visitor interaction type with respect to any suitable input component s and or sensing component s of any suitable smart device or devices of environment e.g. a visitor s audible communication via a microphone of doorbell or selection of an option on a touchscreen user interface of doorbell via touching that touchscreen may be processed and handled in any suitable manner by platform for filtering any undesirable or otherwise annoying visitor interactions while also appropriately detecting certain visitor interactions that maybe leveraged for adjusting the urgency or uniqueness or any other suitable tone of an attempted communication by platform to a system user in response to such detecting.

As described above platform may be operative to disable a functionality of a user interface or doorbell button input component of a smart doorbell for any suitable reason e.g. based on any suitable settings or inferences etc. . For example a message may be conveyed to the visitor that the doorbell input component has been disabled thereby discouraging the visitor from even attempting to functionally interact with the doorbell input component e.g. through the visitor depressing or ringing the doorbell . Alternatively or additionally whether or not it is conveyed to the visitor that a functionality of a doorbell input component is disabled platform may be operative to prevent contacting a system user in certain manners or at all in response to an interaction of any visitor with that doorbell input component under certain system circumstances e.g. if the visitor interacts with the doorbell input component before providing the smart environment with any requested visitor identification information and or visitor intent information . This may be considered whitelisting as platform may be operative to require that certain requirements be met before enabling the functionality of the doorbell input component for a visitor generally e.g. before platform may be operative to generate any system user notifications in response to any visitor interaction with that doorbell input component such as determining a specific identification of the visitor and or at least determining whether the visitor is trusted or untrusted.

Alternatively or additionally platform may be operative to prevent contacting a system user in certain manners or at all in response to an interaction of a particular visitor with that doorbell input component e.g. if a particular visitor has been determined to interact with environment e.g. doorbell in a manner that is undesirable to a system user. This may be considered blacklisting as platform may be operative to prevent certain visitor interaction by a certain visitor from being communicated as system user notification which may be done whether the certain visitor is determined to be trusted or untrusted. Therefore platform may be operative to enable a system user to easily blacklist a particular visitor during a particular mode of smart environment e.g. by defining a mode setting such that certain or all interactions by that particular visitor with environment e.g. with doorbell button may not result in a system user notification that might otherwise be generated by platform for a non blacklisted visitor interacting in the same manner. A blacklisted visitor may be detected like any other suitable visitor e.g. as described above with respect to steps . For example any suitable fingerprint or signature of a visitor may be identified e.g. through facial recognition receipt of affirmatively provided visitor identification detection of an NFC or RFID tag for that particular visitor Wi Fi pairing signals or any other suitable signals that may be detected from a visitor personal device and analyzed by platform etc. .

Platform may be operative to blacklist a visitor or at least certain visitor interactions of a visitor in any suitable way e.g. based on inferences or system user instructions . For example in some embodiments platform may be operative to record a log e.g. as home data that may include a listing of the identity e.g. general or specific of some or all of the visitors detected each day at environment as well as a listing of any interaction each visitor may have had with environment e.g. Visitor A pressed doorbell button of doorbell at front door five times within a ten second period starting at 3 45 15 PM on Tuesday . Platform may be operative to provide such a log for review by a system user of environment such that the system user may select certain visitors or certain interactions of certain visitors to be added to a blacklist whereby going forward platform may be operative to prevent such visitors or such interactions of such visitors from resulting in the generation of system user notifications e.g. via a smart device output component proximate the system user . Once a particular visitor e.g. all interactions by Visitor A and or a particular visitor interaction e.g. an interaction by Visitor A that includes pressing doorbell button more than once within a ten second period has been blacklisted platform may be operative to handle such a blacklisting in any suitable manner when detected. For example in response to detecting a blacklisted interaction platform may be operative to convey a message to the visitor e.g. via speaker or projector or otherwise that such an interaction will not be recognized by a system user and that discourages such behavior going forward. The message may include a customized message from the system user as to why the interaction has been blacklisted and what may be a preferable alternative.

As just one real world example there may be an overly enthusiastic mailman deliverer DL that always presses doorbell button when he or she delivers the mail each day despite a system user s requests to the contrary e.g. because user notifications provided in response to such doorbell presses inevitably wake up a napping child within environment . After 2 3 days of this same activity platform may be operative to recognize e.g. at steps that the same Wi Fi pairing signal is sensed when doorbell button is pressed each day and platform may be operative to store such data in a suitable log by identifying different interactions on different days as being provided by the same visitor. Later after the third day or so the angry homeowner system user may be enabled by platform to review that log and realize that this same visitor was the doorbell ringer at these offending times and then blacklist that visitor. Notably in one embodiment the actual identity of the blacklisted may not be specifically established or revealed by platform in the log and such a visitor may simply be identified in the log as Visitor A or Visitor whose Wi Fi beacon is XYZ . However in other embodiments the actual identity of one or more visitors may be provided in such a log e.g. through any suitable technique described herein such as comparing any detected visitor signature data to one or more databases available to platform .

Such a log may be leveraged by platform for any suitable purpose. For example rather than identifying a particular visitor or a particular visitor interaction in the log for blacklisting that visitor or interaction for preventing future system user notifications in response thereto platform may be operative to assign a particular type of system user notification to a particular visitor or particular visitor interaction identified via a log or otherwise such that such a particular type of system user notification may be utilized by platform in the future in response to detecting such a particular visitor or particular visitor interaction. For example platform may be operative to enable a certain audible message type e.g. a particular ringtones to be provided by platform as at least a portion of a system user notification in response to a future detection of a particular visitor or a particular visitor interaction e.g. to associate a melodic version of the shave and a haircut two bits riff with a particular rhythmic interaction by a visitor of that same shave and a haircut two bits riff.

It is understood that the steps shown in process of are merely illustrative and that existing steps may be modified or omitted additional steps may be added and the order of certain steps may be altered.

Platform may be operative to provide any suitable feedback to a visitor in response to any suitable visitor interaction with environment where such feedback provided to the visitor in response to the visitor interaction may or may not be similar to any communication attempt provided to a system user in response to the visitor interaction. In some embodiments when no audible communication attempt is provided to a system user within environment e.g. when such a communication attempt is done electronically as a text message to a system user device or as a visual only blinking light communication attempt via a smart device within environment e.g. when the system user may be putting a baby down for a nap or is on a telephone call and or when no communication attempt is provided within environment whatsoever e.g. when platform has determined that there is no occupancy within environment and or each occupant is in a do not disturb mode platform may still be operative to generate audible feedback or any other suitable form of feedback to the visitor which may provide the visitor with some sort of confidence that its interaction is being handled by environment . As just one example if platform determined that environment is in a do not disturb mode whereby no audible communication attempt to a system user is generated in response to a visitor interaction e.g. if platform instead only generates a silent communication within environment to a system user that may be attempting to put a baby down for a nap in response to a visitor interaction platform may still be operative to generate visitor feedback that may be audible by the visitor e.g. external to structure outside door in response to a visitor interaction. Such visitor feedback may be sensed and interpreted by the visitor as if it is hearing the same audible output that is being provided to a system user within environment e.g. internal to structure whether or not such an audible output is being provided to a system user within environment . For example such an audible output may be provided by doorbell e.g. audio speaker and or by an audio speaker of another smart device that may be positioned within structure just adjacent internal side of door e.g. within a user handle portion of doorknob where such an audible output may not disturb any system user within structure . As another example an audible output may be generated by platform that may be sensed and interpreted by the visitor as if a dog is barking from within environment in response to the visitor interaction and any attempted user communication. For example if a real dog may be present within environment platform may be operative to generate any suitable output that may instigate such a dog to bark e.g. by generating a dog whistle high pitch sound that may not be detectable by any system user or the visitor but that may excite a dog to bark . Alternatively a sound may be generated and output by any suitable device of environment that may mimic a dog bark.

Platform may be operative to provide different visitor feedback based on occupancy status and or visitor type. For example if platform attempts to communicate with a system user local to or remote from environment in response to a visitor interaction with environment platform may be operative to provide different feedback to the visitor dependent upon whether or not the visitor has been detected as a known or unknown visitor. If the visitor is currently unknown to platform or is otherwise considered a stranger with respect to environment or is otherwise to be treated with a heightened form of security platform may be operative to generate visitor feedback that may be sensed or otherwise interpreted by the visitor as indicative of some form of occupancy at environment e.g. turning on a light within structure or outdoor lighting external to structure or generating an audible dog bark or other suitable noise etc. . By generating such visitor feedback in response to such an unknown visitor interacting with environment e.g. ringing doorbell button platform may be operative to increase the security of environment by making environment seem occupied in some way to the visitor even if environment may currently be unoccupied or in a do not disturb mode. As mentioned above platform may be operative to provide such security enhancing feedback in response to any suitable visitor interaction with environment and not just in response to a visitor interaction with a doorbell button of doorbell . For example in some embodiments platform may be operative to turn on a light within or outside of structure or adjust the functionality of any other suitable device of environment for enhancing the security of environment when any potential visitor e.g. known or unknown is at least initially detected at environment e.g. when environment is in a do not disturb mode or otherwise . Alternatively such security enhancing functionality of platform may be carried out in response to a visitor being detected but then not actively interacting with environment e.g. when the presence of a visitor is detected but then that visitor does not provide requested information to doorbell or otherwise interact with a user interface of doorbell whereby platform may be operative to deem such visitor non interaction as suspicious. As another example such security enhancing functionality of platform may be carried out in response to a visitor actively interacting with environment in an unapproved manner e.g. in response to a visitor attempting to open door through interaction with doorknob before platform has granted such access whereby platform may be operative to deem such visitor interaction as suspicious.

However if the visitor is currently known to platform or otherwise meets any suitable trust threshold with respect to environment or is otherwise not to be treated with a heightened form of security platform may be operative to generate visitor feedback that may be sensed or otherwise interpreted by the visitor as indicative of the fact that platform is currently attempting to contact a system user without necessarily implying occupancy at environment e.g. by conveying a visitor feedback message like please wait while user contact is attempted or please enjoy this hold music as a user is notified of your presence . By generating such visitor feedback in response to such a known visitor interacting with environment e.g. ringing doorbell button platform may be operative to share with the visitor the actual current status of the attempted communication between platform and a system user rather than generating a decoy feedback that may not fool a visitor familiar with environment e.g. whether or not environment would include a barking dog .

It is understood that the steps shown in process of are merely illustrative and that existing steps may be modified or omitted additional steps may be added and the order of certain steps may be altered.

Platform may be operative to leverage any suitable data that may be sensed by any suitable smart device of environment for enhancing the security or convenience of environment . Additionally or alternatively to sensing data that may be indicative of the physical presence identity and or intent of a visitor and or a smart invitation or package label at environment one or more sensing components of one or more smart devices of environment e.g. doorbell may be operative to sense any other suitable data that may be utilized by platform in enhancing the security and or convenience of system users of environment in any suitable ways.

Doorbell and or any other smart device of environment e.g. outdoor lighting gated entry doorknob safe appliance entry detectors etc. may include one or more sensing components that may be operative to measure one or more characteristics for determining the quality of the air or any other similar detectable entity of the external environment of environment e.g. external to structure . For example one or more sensing components of doorbell positioned external to structure may be similar to any suitable sensing component of a hazard detector device positioned within structure or otherwise for measuring air quality and or detecting harmful VOCs and or patent harmful gases particulate dust pollen mold or the like of the environment external to structure . Such external environment data sensed by doorbell or any other suitable smart device or by any other data source of platform e.g. a third party air quality business may be leveraged by platform in combination with any other suitable data for adjusting a platform functionality e.g. a functionality of a smart device of environment or for reporting to any suitable entity for analysis . For example the detected air purity within a particular area or the entirety of structure e.g. as may be sensed by one or more hazard detector devices may be compared by platform e.g. by system or any suitable processing component local to environment with the detected air purity outside of structure e.g. as may be sensed by doorbell or otherwise to control a functionality of a smart device of environment . As a particular example if the outside air is purer than the inside air then platform may be operative to instruct a smart thermostat device to open a vent to permit fresh air into structure otherwise platform may be operative to instruct a thermostat device to recirculate air within structure and to not draw in outside air. Additionally or alternatively as another particular example platform may be operative to send detailed information about the air quality within and external to structure to a mobile personal device user device or other suitable smart device of a user which may help the user identify which pollen or other air impurity may be the culprit of any allergies that the user may be experiencing. As one other example platform may be operative to send an alert to a system user when cigarette smoke is detected by any suitable external sensor e.g. to catch a child attempting to sneak a cigarette outside front door . As another example platform may be operative to aggregate air quality data received from multiple environments in various geographic locations or other suitable groupings and to provide for example smog alerts pollen warnings etc. of those groupings to any suitable entity e.g. weather reporting business entities . As another example platform may be operative to compare detected external and or internal air quality of different areas of environment with one another at a specific time or historically e.g. by time of day day of week season of year etc. for identifying certain areas that may have issues to be addressed e.g. a corner of structure that is exposed to significantly more pollen than other portions of environment during the Spring and may benefit from additional filtration or inspection of flora and fauna near that area at that time . As another example platform may be operative to compare detected external and or internal air quality of environment with other smart environments. Any one or more of such comparisons or data aggregations with respect to air quality of one or more internal or external areas of environment may be stored for and or shared with certain entities such as prospective buyers of environment e.g. at real estate business entity for determining whether such qualities of environment are suitable. Additionally or alternatively any other weather phenomena or characteristic of the air quality e.g. temperature humidity wind levels e.g. strength speed of the movement of the air wind direction e.g. direction of the movement of the air etc. may be detected e.g. by any sensing component s doorbell at environment e.g. internal to and or ambient of structure and utilized similarly to any air purity levels described above. For example the outside humidity and temperature data may be compared with or considered by a thermostat when controlling the HVAC to best accomplish the occupants desired comfort preferences. Further for example this information may be presented to the occupants through a number of user interfaces such as a user interface associated with another one of the devices located inside of the home the television mobile and other computing devices or audibly. In some instances platform e.g. system may collect such weather data from multiple smart environments across a plurality of geographic locations or other suitable groupings and such aggregated weather data may be sold or otherwise provided to weather services e.g. any suitable business entity or may be used to provide weather data to smart home occupants or potential buyers.

Doorbell and or any other smart device of environment e.g. outdoor lighting gated entry doorknob safe appliance entry detectors etc. may include one or more sensing components that may be operative to measure one or more characteristics for determining noise of the external environment of environment e.g. external to structure . For example one or more sensing components of doorbell e.g. microphone may be positioned external to structure for sensing any suitable noise external to structure . Such ambient noise data sensed by doorbell or any other suitable smart device or by any other data source of platform e.g. a third party noise detection business may be leveraged by platform in combination with any other suitable data for adjusting a platform functionality e.g. a functionality of a smart device of environment or for reporting to any suitable entity for analysis . For example the detected noise levels within a particular area or the entirety of structure e.g. as may be sensed by one or more hazard detectors may be compared by platform e.g. by system or any suitable processing component local to environment with the noise levels outside of structure e.g. as may be sensed by doorbell or otherwise to control a functionality of a smart device of environment . As a particular example if the noise level outside of structure significantly spikes e.g. due to a helicopter hovering overhead then platform may be operative to instruct a smart appliance e.g. a television or smart hazard detector device or any other suitable smart device to increase its volume output level to overcome or otherwise compensate for the additional ambient noise pollution e.g. so a system user may still hear important warnings or other communications from such smart devices . As another example platform may be operative to analyze ambient noise detected at environment e.g. by doorbell to determine that a street adjacent to structure may meet a threshold level of traffic where such a determination may result in one or more inferences being made by platform about the safety of any children currently occupying environment e.g. Child playing outside of structure at environment of . For example platform may be operative to trigger any suitable alarm e.g. at environment such as with a hazard detector within structure in the event one or more of the children are detected by the occupancy sensing to be outside of the home during such a detected traffic event. Such an alert may enable a parent or other caretaker at environment e.g. Husband within structure to quickly take action to protect the child from the detected traffic of course other suitable environment detectors such as a camera and or motion detector alone or in combination with such a noise sensor may also enable platform to facilitate such a security feature . Additionally or alternatively as another particular example platform may be operative to send detailed information about the noise levels within and external to structure to a mobile personal device user device or other suitable smart device of a user which may help the user identify which areas of environment may be experiencing more problematic noise issues. As another example platform may be operative to aggregate noise data received from multiple environments in various geographic locations or other suitable groupings and to provide for example noise pollution reports of those groupings to any suitable entity e.g. law enforcement entities . As another example platform may be operative to compare detected external and or internal noise levels of different areas of environment with one another at a specific time or historically e.g. by time of day day of week season of year etc. for identifying certain areas that may have issues to be addressed e.g. a corner of structure that is exposed to significantly more noise than other portions of environment at certain times of day and may benefit from additional sound proofing or noise filtration or other accommodations . As another example platform may be operative to compare detected external and or noise levels of environment with other smart environments. Any one or more of such comparisons or data aggregations with respect to noise levels of one or more internal or external areas of environment may be stored for and or shared with certain entities such as prospective buyers of environment e.g. at a real estate agent business for determining whether such qualities of environment are suitable. Additionally or alternatively any motion levels or other suitable activity may be detected e.g. by any sensing component s doorbell at environment e.g. internal to and ambient of structure and utilized similarly to any noise levels described above e.g. a combination of detected motion and noise levels may be leveraged to detect a traffic threshold for enabling platform to initiate an alarm for protecting any children of environment or motion levels may be detected to indicate a stranger casing environment for potential theft or an animal wandering in the backyard etc. . Additionally or alternatively any ambient light levels or other suitable ambient conditions may be detected e.g. by any sensing component s doorbell at environment e.g. internal to and ambient of structure and utilized similarly to any noise levels described above.

As described above e.g. with respect to detected air quality any suitable data indicative of any suitable characteristic or phenomena external to structure e.g. noise levels activity levels ambient light levels weather etc. that may be detectable by doorbell or any other suitable data source of platform may be analyzed in any suitable manner e.g. with respect to any other suitable data for leveraging in any suitable way. As one particular example any suitable detected ambient data of structure may be compared with any suitable internal data of environment or analyzed on its own or with respect to any other suitable data for adjusting a platform functionality such as for adjusting a functionality of a smart device and or for adjusting a mode or mode setting enabled or to be enabled e.g. ambient detected noise e.g. by a microphone sensing component of doorbell may be leveraged to adjust the volume level of audio output by a smart device within structure e.g. from a smart hazard detector device or any suitable controllable device such as a stereo for dynamically tuning such internal volume to overcome any ambient noise sources . Additionally or alternatively as another particular example platform may be operative to send detailed information about the detected value of certain ambient conditions of environment to a mobile personal device user device or other suitable smart device of a user which may help the user identify when and where certain noises are coming from. As another example platform may be operative to aggregate ambient data received from multiple environments in various geographic locations or other suitable groupings and to provide for example air pollution reports of those groupings to any suitable entity e.g. law enforcement entities . As another example platform may be operative to compare detected external and or internal phenomena from different areas of environment with one another at a specific time or historically e.g. by time of day day of week season of year etc. for identifying certain areas that may have issues to be addressed e.g. a corner of structure that is exposed to significantly more noise pollution than other portions of environment at a specific time of day and may benefit from additional sound proofing . As another example platform may be operative to compare detected external and or internal phenomena of environment with other smart environments. Any one or more of such comparisons or data aggregations with respect to detected phenomena e.g. air quality noise levels activity e.g. motion levels ambient light levels weather etc. of one or more internal or external areas of environment may be stored for and or shared with certain entities such as prospective buyers of environment for determining whether such qualities of environment are suitable.
